# Russian Civil War Events

add_namespace = rcw_usfev

# Восстание забайкальских казаков (мятеж Семёнова)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.1
	title = rcw_usfev.1.t
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.1.desc
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = radical_socialism
				has_government = communism
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_all_russian_constituent_assembly_second_session_serfdom }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.1.desc_1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = radical_socialism
				has_government = communism
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_all_russian_constituent_assembly_second_session_serfdom }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.1.desc_2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_all_russian_constituent_assembly_second_session_serfdom
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_rus_kazaks_war
	
	trigger = {
		has_start_date < 1917.11.7
		tag = RUS
		BKL = { exists = no }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = BKL_revolt }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_cossacks_were_disbanded }
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 77299 } set_nationality = BKL }
			BKL = {
				#transfer_state = 761
				#transfer_state = 1209
				transfer_state = 950
				#transfer_state = 951
				add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
				remove_all_foreing_locked_templates_from_liberated_country = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								tag = PREV
								is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
								former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes
								has_war_with = PREV
								is_in_faction_with = PREV
							}
						}
						set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_provisional_government_not_so_provisional }
				BKL = { load_focus_tree = Transbaikal_white_cossaks_late_focus transfer_state = 563 }
				else = {
					BKL = {
						remove_ideas = peasant_and_land_and_bread_question_0_5
						add_ideas = marching_army_idea
						set_cosmetic_tag = BKL_SMS
					}
				}
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Kazach'ya brigada"
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1.a
		set_country_flag = BKL_revolt
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_provisional_government_not_so_provisional }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = BKL
				type = annex_everything
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				BKL = {
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 100
						producer = JAP
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = artillery_equipment
						amount = 24
						producer = JAP
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Pekhotniy batalyon"
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						}
						support = {
							artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 100
						producer = FNG
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Miliceyskiy batalyon"
						regiments = {
							militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						}
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Kavaleriyskaya brigada"
						regiments = {
							cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						}
					}
					add_manpower = 2000
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 200
						producer = BKL
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Kavaleriyskaya brigada"
						regiments = {
							cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						}
					}
					capital_scope = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Yaponskiy pekhotniy otryad\" division_template = \"Pekhotniy batalyon\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.01 "
							owner = ROOT
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Kitayskaya miliciya\" division_template = \"Miliceyskiy batalyon\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.01 "
							owner = ROOT
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Kitayskaya miliciya\" division_template = \"Miliceyskiy batalyon\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.01 "
							owner = ROOT
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Mongolskaya brigada\" division_template = \"Kavaleriyskaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.01 start_equipment_factor = 1"
							owner = ROOT
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Otryad hunhuzov\" division_template = \"Kavaleriyskaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.1 start_equipment_factor = 1"
							owner = ROOT
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 500
						producer = BKL
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = artillery_equipment
						amount = 5
						producer = BKL
					}
					add_timed_idea = { idea = BKL_russian_volunteers_idea days = 182 }
					add_timed_idea = { idea = BKL_right_oficers days = 365 }
					add_ideas = BKL_special_manchu_squad_idea
					add_country_leader_trait = ataman
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_capital = { state = 950 }
				if = {
					limit = { RUS = { OR = { has_completed_focus = RUS_struggle_against_counterrevolution NOT = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus } } } }
					RUS = {
						declare_war_on = {
							target = BKL
							type = annex_everything
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1.b
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			OR = {
				has_government = radical_socialism
				has_government = communism

				target = BKL

						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						}

						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

					}

						name = "Miliceyskiy batalyon"
						regiments = {

						}
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Kavaleriyskaya brigada"

					}

					}

							division = "name = \"Yaponskiy pekhotniy otryad\" division_template = \"Pekhotniy batalyon\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.01 "

							division = "name = \"Kitayskaya miliciya\" division_template = \"Miliceyskiy batalyon\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.01 "
							owner = ROOT
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Kitayskaya miliciya\" division_template = \"Miliceyskiy batalyon\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.01 "
							owner = ROOT
						}

							division = "name = \"Mongolskaya brigada\" division_template = \"Kavaleriyskaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.01 start_equipment_factor = 1"
							owner = ROOT

							division = "name = \"Otryad hunhuzov\" division_template = \"Kavaleriyskaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.1 start_equipment_factor = 1"
							owner = ROOT

					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

					}
					add_timed_idea = { idea = BKL_russian_volunteers_idea days = 182 }
					add_timed_idea = { idea = BKL_right_oficers days = 365 }
					add_ideas = BKL_special_manchu_squad_idea
					add_country_leader_trait = ataman
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_capital = { state = 950 }
				if = {
					limit = { RUS = { OR = { has_completed_focus = RUS_struggle_against_counterrevolution NOT = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus } } } }
					RUS = {
						declare_war_on = {
							target = BKL
							type = annex_everything
						}
					}
				}

	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1.c
		trigger = {

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.2
	title = rcw_usfev.2.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.2.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rcw_czech_uprising
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		tag = BKL
		controls_state = 566
		NOT = { owns_state = 566 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.2.a
		transfer_state = 566
		add_state_core = 566
	}
}

###Боевые дружины левых эсеров поднимают восстание, если они в составе КОМУЧ###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.13
	title = rcw_usfev.13.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.13.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rcw_czech_uprising
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CCA
		has_war_with = RUS
		RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		has_country_flag = main_left_essers_is_here
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.13.a
		load_oob = CCA_left_esser_rise
		add_state_core = 398
		add_state_core = 249
		add_state_core = 239
		add_state_core = 250
		add_state_core = 252
		add_state_core = 248
		RUS = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 19189 } set_nationality = CCA } }
	}
	
}

# Свержение советской власти в Поволжье
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.16
	title = rcw_usfev.16.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.16.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_rcw_sibir_uprising
	
	trigger = {
		always = no
		tag = RUS
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = CCA_fired }
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
		OCH = { controls_state = 251 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_equipment_fraction = 0.8
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88147 } set_nationality = CCA }
			add_to_variable = { var = global.RUS_threat_of_intervention value = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_3
					add_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_4
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_2
					add_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_1 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_1
					add_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 329 TAN = { exists = no } }
				release = TAN
			}
		}
	}
	#КОМУЧ нацсиндов
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.16.a
		set_global_flag = CCA_fired
		add_war_support = 0.15
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 652
					state = 407
					state = 406
					state = 1071
				}
			}
			add_core_of = OCH
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						PREV = { is_owned_by = PREV }
					}
				}
				is_core_of = OCH
			}
			OCH = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { OCH = { controls_state = 651 } }
			OCH = {
				transfer_state = 573
				transfer_state = 651
				transfer_state = 1299
				transfer_state = 1072
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 251
					state = 1070
					state = 573
					state = 582
					state = 651
					state = 1299
					state = 1072
					state = 572
					state = 1103
					state = 250
					state = 255
					state = 1100
					state = 1101
					state = 252
					state = 1231
				}
			}
			CCA = { add_state_core = PREV }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						PREV = { is_owned_by = PREV }
					}
				}
				OR = {
					state = 251
					state = 1070
					state = 573
					state = 582
					state = 651
					state = 1299
					state = 1072
					state = 572
					state = 1103
				}
			}
			CCA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		hidden_effect = { DON = { remove_ideas = DON_Peoples_army_presence_idea } }
		CCA = {
			inherit_technology = ROOT
			add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
			remove_all_foreing_locked_templates_from_liberated_country = yes
			load_oob = CCA_1918
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_czechoslovak_legion_uprising OR = { has_country_flag = SOV_czechs_uprising_position_2_1 has_country_flag = SOV_czechs_uprising_position_2_2 } } }
				load_oob = CCA_czechoslovak_corps
				if = {
					limit = { SIB = { exists = yes } }
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_owned_by = ROOT
								is_owned_by = KAZ
								any_country = {
									is_subject_of = ROOT
									PREV = { is_owned_by = PREV }
								}
							}
							OR = {
								state = 516
								state = 824
								state = 566
								state = 567
								state = 568
								state = 569
								state = 1279
								state = 571
								state = 1067
								state = 575
								state = 576
								state = 577
								
								state = 583
								state = 588
								state = 590
							}
						}
						SIB = { transfer_state = PREV }
					}
					SIB = {
						load_oob = SIB_1918
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { SIB = { exists = yes } KAZ = { exists = yes is_subject = no } }
						SIB = { KAZ = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties = yes } }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { SIB = { exists = yes } }
					SIB = {
						declare_war_on = {
							target = ROOT
							type = annex_everything
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_popularities = {
				national_syndicalism = 30
				authoritarism = 2
				social_conservatism = 5
				radical_socialism = 7
				social_democracy = 12
				social_liberalism = 29
				market_liberalism = 10
				communism = 5
			}
			set_politics = { ruling_party = national_syndicalism }
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							tag = PREV
							is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
							former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes
							has_war_with = PREV
							is_in_faction_with = PREV
						}
					}
					set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { KAZ = { exists = yes is_subject = no } }
				CCA = { KAZ = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties = yes } }
			}
		}
		CCA = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SIB = { exists = yes } }
			SIB = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ROOT
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		OCH = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.14 hours = 1 } }
	}
	#КОМУЧ нацсиндов
	option = {
		trigger = {
			CCA = { exists = no }
			is_ai = no
		}
		name = rcw_usfev.16.b
		set_global_flag = CCA_fired
		add_war_support = 0.15
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 652
					state = 407
					state = 406
					state = 1071
				}
			}
			add_core_of = OCH
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						PREV = { is_owned_by = PREV }
					}
				}
				is_core_of = OCH
			}
			OCH = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { OCH = { controls_state = 651 } }
			OCH = {
				transfer_state = 573
				transfer_state = 651
				transfer_state = 1299
				transfer_state = 1072
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 251
					state = 1070
					state = 573
					state = 582
					state = 651
					state = 1299
					state = 1072
					state = 572
					state = 1103
					state = 250
					state = 255
					state = 1100
					state = 1101
					state = 252
					state = 1231
				}
			}
			CCA = { add_state_core = PREV }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						PREV = { is_owned_by = PREV }
					}
				}
				OR = {
					state = 251
					state = 1070
					state = 573
					state = 582
					state = 651
					state = 1299
					state = 1072
					state = 572
					state = 1103
				}
			}
			CCA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		hidden_effect = { DON = { remove_ideas = DON_Peoples_army_presence_idea } }
		CCA = {
			inherit_technology = ROOT
			add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
			remove_all_foreing_locked_templates_from_liberated_country = yes
			load_oob = CCA_1918
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_czechoslovak_legion_uprising OR = { has_country_flag = SOV_czechs_uprising_position_2_1 has_country_flag = SOV_czechs_uprising_position_2_2 } } }
				load_oob = CCA_czechoslovak_corps
				if = {
					limit = { SIB = { exists = yes } }
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_owned_by = ROOT
								is_owned_by = KAZ
								any_country = {
									is_subject_of = ROOT
									PREV = { is_owned_by = PREV }
								}
							}

								state = 516

								state = 590
							}
						}
						SIB = { transfer_state = PREV }
					}
					SIB = {
						load_oob = SIB_1918
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { SIB = { exists = yes } KAZ = { exists = yes is_subject = no } }
						SIB = { KAZ = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties = yes } }
					}
				}
				if = {

				social_conservatism = 5
				radical_socialism = 7
				social_democracy = 12
				social_liberalism = 29

				communism = 5
			}
			set_politics = { ruling_party = national_syndicalism }
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							tag = PREV
							is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
							former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes

							is_in_faction_with = PREV

		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.18.desc_1
		trigger = {
			SOV = { exists = yes OR = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism has_government = social_democracy } }
		}
	}
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_cca_esser

		name = rcw_usfev.18.a

			random_country = {
				limit = { exists = yes has_country_leader = { name = "Vladimir Lenin" ruling_only = yes } }

							factor = 0

						}

							factor = 0.5

							factor = 1.75
							has_completed_focus = RUS_vchk
						}

					}
				}
			}
			
			random_country = {

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.19
	title = rcw_usfev.19.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.19.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rcw_votkinsk_uprising
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		tag = RUS
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
		NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
		any_country = {
			is_main_former_russian_empire_country_without_other_triggers = yes
			has_war_with = RUS
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = IZH_yet_freedom }
		controls_state = 399
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				any_state = {
					region = 40
					NOT = { is_controlled_by = RUS }
				}
				surrender_progress > 0.3
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.05
			OR = {
				399 = {
					any_neighbor_state = {
						CONTROLLER = {
							is_main_former_russian_empire_country_without_other_triggers = yes
							has_war_with = RUS
						}
					}
				}
				surrender_progress > 0.6
			}
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	#is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.19.a
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.RCW_green_var_Russian_SFSR
			value = 1
		}
		set_country_flag = IZH_yet_freedom
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_main_former_russian_empire_country_without_other_triggers = yes
				NOT = { tag = RUS }
				any_state = {
					region = 40
					is_controlled_by = PREV
				}
			}

		}

			transfer_state = 399
			set_cosmetic_tag = IZH

				IZH_tension_with_the_udmurts

				collapse_of_railway_system_1
				peasant_and_land_and_bread_question_0_5
				lack_of_officers_5
			}
			country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.25 days = 1 }
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							tag = PREV
							is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
							former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes
							has_war_with = PREV
							is_in_faction_with = PREV
						}
					}
					set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
				}
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = UDM
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.19.b
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.RCW_green_var_Russian_SFSR
			value = 1
		}
		set_country_flag = IZH_yet_freedom
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_main_former_russian_empire_country_without_other_triggers = yes
				NOT = { tag = RUS }
				any_state = {
					region = 40
					is_controlled_by = PREV
				}
			}

		}
		UDM = {

			set_cosmetic_tag = IZH
			inherit_technology = RUS

				}
			random_other_country = {

					original_tag = CCA
					has_government = radical_socialism
				}
				save_global_event_target_as = CCA_CW
				set_stability = 0.9
				set_war_support = 0.8

						has_war_with = CCA
						NOT = { has_war_with = event_target:CCA_CW }
					}
					declare_war_on = { target = event_target:CCA_CW type = annex_everything }
				}
				event_target:CCA_CW = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							is_in_array = {
								array = unrecognized_states
								value = ROOT.id
							}
						}
						set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = { clear_global_event_target = CCA_CW }
			}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.42
	title = rcw_usfev.42.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.42.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_derber_and_vologodsky
	
	trigger = {
		tag = SIB
		is_subject = no
		NOT = { has_government = communism has_government = radical_socialism }
		has_country_flag = SIB_start_political_instability
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = foreign_minister_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = economy_minister_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = security_minister_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_intel_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = military_minister_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = army_chief
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.42.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_capital = { state = 578 }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberalism
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = despotism
		clr_country_flag = SIB_start_political_instability
		add_ideas = {
			Pyotr_Derber_1
			Pyotr_Vologodsky_2
			Ivan_Mikhailov_3
			Alexander_Novosyolov_4
			Grigoriy_Patushinsky_5
			Arkady_Krakovetsky_6
			Alexey_Almazov_army_chief
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.42.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberalism
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = despotism
		clr_country_flag = SIB_start_political_instability
		add_ideas = {
			Pyotr_Vologodsky_1
			Pyotr_Vologodsky_2
			Ivan_Mikhailov_3
			Vladimir_Krutovsky_4
			Grigoriy_Patushinsky_5
			Alexey_Almazov_6
			Alexey_Almazov_army_chief
		}
	}
}

# Сибирский ультиматум о передаче Челябинска, контроля над Уральским правительством, аннексии (КОМУЧ)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.44
	title = rcw_usfev.44.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.44.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rus_entente

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.44.a
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { SIB_pressure_CCA = 1 } }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = SIB modifier = SIB_accept_CCA }
			SIB = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = CCA modifier = SIB_accept }
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.46 days = 1 }
			}
			if = {
			limit = { URL = { exists = yes is_subject_of = SIB } }
			URL = {
				transfer_state = 572
				}
				else = {
					SIB = {
						transfer_state = 572
						add_state_core = 572
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { SIB_pressure_CCA = 2 } }
			SIB = {
				URL = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_integrated_puppet = yes }
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.46 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { SIB_pressure_CCA = 3 } }
			CCA = {
				every_unit_leader = {
						set_nationality = SIB
					}
			}
			SIB = {
				annex_country = {
					target = CCA
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = CCA }
					add_core_of = SIB
				}
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.46 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.44.b
		SIB = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.45 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}
	}
}

# Мир с Сибирью aka Мир с советами
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.50
	title = rcw_usfev.50.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.50.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_moscow_peace
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.50.a
		set_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_reds_n_Siberia_peace
		if = {
			limit = { SIB = { is_in_faction = yes is_faction_leader = no } }
			every_country = {
				limit = { OR = { tag = SIB is_subject_of = SIB } }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = RSR
					is_subject_of = RSR
				}
				capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } }
			}
			RSR = { end_puppet = PREV }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		RSR = {
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = { OR = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } } tag = SIB is_subject_of = SIB is_in_faction_with = SIB } OR = { is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes former_russian_empire_polish_region_country = yes } OR = { is_subject = no OVERLORD = { OR = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } } tag = SIB is_subject_of = SIB is_in_faction_with = SIB } OR = { is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes former_russian_empire_polish_region_country = yes } } } }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 }
						OWNER = {
							OR = {
								tag = RSR
								AND = {
									is_subject_of = RSR
									NOT = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } } }
								}
								AND = {
									is_in_faction_with = RSR
									NOT = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } } }
								}
							}
						}
						is_controlled_by = PREV
					}
					remove_core_of = OWNER
					remove_core_of = RSR
					PREV = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = { OR = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } } tag = SIB is_subject_of = SIB is_in_faction_with = SIB } OR = { is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes former_russian_empire_polish_region_country = yes } NOT = { is_main_former_russian_empire_country = yes } OR = { is_subject = no OVERLORD = { OR = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } } tag = SIB is_subject_of = SIB is_in_faction_with = SIB } OR = { is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes former_russian_empire_polish_region_country = yes } } } }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 }
						OWNER = {
							OR = {
								tag = RSR
								AND = {
									is_subject_of = RSR
									NOT = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } } }
								}
								AND = {
									is_in_faction_with = RSR
									NOT = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } } }
								}
							}
						}
						is_core_of = PREV
						CONTROLLER = { OR = { tag = RSR NOT = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV } } }
					}
					remove_core_of = OWNER
					remove_core_of = RSR
					PREV = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		SIB = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OWNER = {
						OR = {
							tag = RSR
							AND = {
								is_subject_of = RSR
								NOT = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } } }
							}
							AND = {
								is_in_faction_with = RSR
								NOT = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } } }
							}
						}
					}
					OR = {
						region = 14
						region = 87
						region = 147
						region = 148
						region = 149
						region = 151
						region = 152
						region = 154
						region = 155
						region = 186
						region = 229
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = OWNER
				remove_core_of = RSR
				SIB = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		
		RSR = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OWNER = {
						OR = {
							tag = SIB
							is_subject_of = SIB
							is_in_faction_with = SIB
							AND = {
								has_war_with = RSR
								capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } }
							}
						}
					}
					is_on_continent = europe
					NOT = {
						region = 137
						state = 398
						state = 651
						state = 1299
						state = 1270
						state = 399
						state = 1099
						state = 249
						state = 251
						state = 401
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = OWNER
				remove_core_of = SIB
				RSR = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { SIB = { controls_state = 251 } }
			SIB = {
				add_political_power = -500
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OWNER = {
						OR = {
							tag = RSR
							is_subject_of = RSR
							is_in_faction_with = RSR
						}
					}
					OR = {
						region = 136
						region = 137
						region = 138
						region = 232
						state = 398
						state = 651
						state = 1299
						state = 1270
						state = 399
						state = 1099
						state = 249
						state = 251
						state = 401
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = OWNER
				remove_core_of = RSR
				SIB = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = RSR
						is_subject_of = RSR
					}
					capital_scope = { OR = { region = 136 region = 137 region = 138 region = 232 state = 398 state = 651 state = 1299 state = 1299 state = 1270 state = 399 state = 1099 state = 249 state = 251 state = 401 } }
				}
				RSR = { end_puppet = PREV }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { SIB = { controls_state = 651 controls_state = 652 } }
			SIB = {
				add_political_power = -200
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = RSR
					OR = {
						region = 136
						region = 138
						region = 232
						
						state = 398
						state = 651
						state = 1299
						state = 1270
						state = 652
						state = 1072
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = RSR
				SIB = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = RSR
						is_subject_of = RSR
					}
					capital_scope = { OR = { region = 136 region = 138 region = 232 state = 398 state = 651 state = 1299 state = 1270 state = 652 state = 1072 } }
				}
				RSR = { end_puppet = PREV }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			RSR = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OWNER = {
							OR = {
								tag = SIB
								is_subject_of = SIB
								is_in_faction_with = SIB
								AND = {
									has_war_with = RSR
									capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 region = 136 region = 138 region = 232 state = 398 state = 651 state = 1299 state = 1270 state = 652 state = 1072 } }
								}
							}
						}
						OR = {
							region = 40
							region = 137
							region = 231
						}
						NOT = {
							state = 398
							state = 651
							state = 1299
							state = 1270
							state = 652
							state = 1072
						}
					}
					remove_core_of = OWNER
					remove_core_of = SIB
					RSR = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { SIB = { controls_state = 572 controls_state = 653 } }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OWNER = {
						OR = {
							tag = RSR
							is_subject_of = RSR
							is_in_faction_with = RSR
						}
					}
					OR = {
						state = 1025
						state = 653
						state = 1067
						state = 572
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = OWNER
				remove_core_of = RSR
				SIB = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = RSR
						is_subject_of = RSR
					}
					capital_scope = { OR = { state = 1025 state = 653 state = 1067 state = 572 } }
				}
				RSR = { end_puppet = PREV }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			RSR = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OWNER = {
							OR = {
								tag = SIB
								is_subject_of = SIB
								is_in_faction_with = SIB
								AND = {
									has_war_with = RSR
									capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 region = 136 state = 1025 state = 653 state = 1067 state = 572 state = 589 } NOT = { state = 402 } }
								}
							}
						}
						OR = {
							region = 40
							region = 137
							region = 231
							region = 232
							state = 402
						}
						NOT = {
							state = 1025
							state = 653
							state = 1067
							state = 572
							state = 589
						}
					}
					remove_core_of = OWNER
					remove_core_of = SIB
					RSR = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
			give_military_access = SIB
			give_guarantee = SIB
			SIB = {
				add_political_power = -50
				if = {
					limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
					dismantle_faction = yes
				}
				every_country = { limit = { is_subject_of = SIB } OVERLORD = { end_puppet = PREV } }
				add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
				remove_ideas_with_trait = trade_laws
				add_ideas = free_trade
				add_ideas = SIB_hard_peace_idea
				give_military_access = RSR
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = SIB
						is_subject_of = SIB
					}
				}
				SIB = { end_puppet = PREV }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			give_military_access = SIB
			give_guarantee = SIB
			SIB = {
				add_political_power = -50
				if = {
					limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
					dismantle_faction = yes
				}
				every_country = { limit = { is_subject_of = SIB } OVERLORD = { end_puppet = PREV } }
				add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
				remove_ideas_with_trait = trade_laws
				add_ideas = free_trade
				add_ideas = SIB_hard_peace_idea
				give_military_access = RSR
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = SIB
						is_subject_of = SIB
					}
				}
				SIB = { end_puppet = PREV }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			RSR = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OWNER = {
							OR = {
								tag = SIB
								is_subject_of = SIB
								is_in_faction_with = SIB
								AND = {
									has_war_with = RSR
									capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } }
								}
							}
						}
						OR = {
							region = 40
							region = 136
							region = 137
							region = 138
							region = 231
							region = 232
						}
					}
					remove_core_of = OWNER
					remove_core_of = SIB
					RSR = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		
		RSR = {
			every_enemy_country = { limit = { OR = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } } tag = SIB is_subject_of = SIB is_in_faction_with = SIB } OR = { is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes former_russian_empire_polish_region_country = yes } OR = { is_subject = no OVERLORD = { OR = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } } tag = SIB is_subject_of = SIB is_in_faction_with = SIB } OR = { is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes former_russian_empire_polish_region_country = yes } } } } white_peace = RSR }
		}
		diplomatic_relation = { country = SIB relation = non_aggression_pact }
		SIB = { diplomatic_relation = { country = RSR relation = non_aggression_pact } }
		
		
		every_state = { limit = { is_owned_by = SIB } remove_core_of = RSR remove_claim_by = RSR }
		every_state = { limit = { is_owned_by = RSR } remove_core_of = SIB remove_claim_by = SIB }
		
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.50.b

						add_war_support = -0.05
						add_political_power = -50
						}
			}
	}
}

		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservatism popularity = 0.07 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.54.b
		if = { limit = { any_unit_leader = { has_id = 92345 } } every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 92345 } } set_nationality = SCH } }
		retire_ideology_leader = despotism
		set_country_flag = Alexey_Almazov_dismissed
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = Alexey_Almazov_6 }
			remove_ideas = Alexey_Almazov_6
			add_ideas = Pavel_Rinov_6
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = Alexey_Almazov_army_chief }
			remove_ideas = Alexey_Almazov_army_chief
			add_ideas = Pavel_Rinov_army_chief
		}
		every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 92353 is_field_marshal = no } promote_leader = yes }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.55
	title = rcw_usfev.55.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.55.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_military_coup
	
	trigger = {
		tag = SIB
		OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = { has_government = social_liberalism has_government = social_democracy }
				check_variable = { authoritarian_parties > 0.3 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_government = market_liberalism
				check_variable = { authoritarian_parties > 0.35 }
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_government = social_conservatism
			has_government = authoritarism
			has_government = despotism
			has_government = fascism
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.55.a #Гришин
		trigger = { has_country_leader = { name = "Alexey Grishin-Almazov" ruling_only = no } }
		set_politics = { ruling_party = despotism }
		add_ideas = military_dictatorship_gov_form
		add_stability = -0.15
		add_war_support = 0.02
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberalism popularity = -0.25 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberalism popularity = -0.1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = despotism popularity = 0.05 }
		add_ideas = RSS_atamanshina

		country_event = rcw_usfev.58
	}

		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberalism popularity = -0.1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = national_syndicalism popularity = 0.05 }
		add_ideas = RSS_atamanshina
		country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.57 days = 2 }

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.60
	title = rcw_usfev.60.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.60.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_ungern_WAAAR
	
	trigger = {
		tag = TAN
		has_country_flag = Ungren_SIB
		OR = {
			MON = { exists = no }
			AND = {
				controls_state = 330
				MON = { exists = yes }
			}
			MON = { is_subject_of = TAN }
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.60.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = MON
				OR = {
					tag = TAN
					AND = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction_with = TAN
					}
				}
			}
			white_peace = MON
		}
		if = {
			limit = {SIB = {exists = yes} NOT = {SIB = {has_government = communism has_government = radical_socialism}}}
			SIB = {annex_country = { target = TAN transfer_troops = yes }}
			MON = {
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Bogdo-gegen VIII"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/empety.dds"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = monarchism
					traits = {}
				}
				TAN = {
					every_unit_leader = {
						set_nationality = MON
					}
				}
			}
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77402 } } set_nationality = SIB }
			set_politics = {ruling_party = authoritarism}
			change_tag_from = SIB
			else = {
				TAN = {
					every_unit_leader = {
						set_nationality = MON
					}
				}
				MON = {
					annex_country = { target = TAN transfer_troops = yes }
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Roman Fyodorovich von Ungern-Sternberg"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Roman_Fyodorovich_von_Ungern-Sternberg.dds"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = monarchism
						traits = { spirit_of_genghis warmonger_old_general }
					}
				}
				change_tag_from = MON
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.60.b
		trigger = {SIB = {exists = yes} NOT = {SIB = {has_government = communism has_government = radical_socialism}}}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = MON
				OR = {
					tag = TAN
					AND = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction_with = TAN
					}
				}
			}
			white_peace = MON
		}
		SIB = {annex_country = { target = TAN transfer_troops = yes }}
		MON = {
		create_country_leader = {
		name = "Bogdo-gegen VIII"
		picture = "gfx/leaders/empety.dds"
		expire = "1965.1.1"
		ideology = monarchism
		traits = {}
		}
		TAN = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				set_nationality = MON
			}
		}
		}
		every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77402 } } set_nationality = SIB }
		set_politics = {ruling_party = authoritarism}
		change_tag_from = MON
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_sovarmy

		tag = SIB
		always = no
		surrender_progress > 0.4
		RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired }
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = { name = "Alexandr Kolchak" }
			has_country_leader = { name = "Roman Fyodorovich von Ungern-Sternberg" }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 20
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.72.a
		#news_event
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				set_politics = {ruling_party = despotism elections_allowed = no}
				set_party_name = { ideology = despotism long_name = RUS_authoritarism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_authoritarism_kolchak_party }
				create_country_leader = { name = "Alexandr Kolchak" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Alexandr_Kolchak_supreme_ruler.dds" expire = "1936.2.7" ideology = despotism_ideology traits = { moy_admiral warmonger_old_general goal_in_politics goal } }
				hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = news_n.30 days = 1 } }
			}
			50 = {
				add_political_power = -50
			}
		}
	}
	
}

# Восстание Политцентра (только Сибирь)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.73
	title = rcw_usfev.73.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.73.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sovarmy
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		tag = SIB
		RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RCW_Politcenter_fired }
		surrender_progress > 0.7
		NOT = { has_government = social_liberalism }
		NOT = { has_government = social_democracy }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = RCW_Politcenter_fired
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.73.a
		#news_event
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB }
				create_country_leader = { name = "Florian Fyodorovich" desc = "RUS_Florian_Fyodorovich_DESC" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Florian_Fyodorovich.dds" ideology = social_democracy_ideology traits = {  } }
				else = {
					create_country_leader = { name = "Florian Fyodorovich" desc = "RUS_Florian_Fyodorovich_DESC" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Florian_Fyodorovich.dds" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = {  } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { controls_state = 566 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB }
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = social_democracy
					size = 0.1
					capital = 566
					states = {
						566
					}
				}
				else = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = social_liberalism
						size = 0.1
						capital = 566
						states = {
							566
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { controls_state = 571 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB }
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = social_democracy
						size = 0.1
						capital = 571
						states = {
							571
						}
					}
					else = {
						start_civil_war = {
							ideology = social_liberalism
							size = 0.1
							capital = 571
							states = {
								571
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB }
						start_civil_war = {
							ideology = social_democracy
							size = 0.1
						}
						else = {
							start_civil_war = {
								ideology = social_liberalism
								size = 0.1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = ROOT
						OR = {
							has_government = social_democracy
							has_government = social_liberalism
						}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = Politcenter
					save_global_event_target_as = Politcenter
					set_stability = 0.9
					set_war_support = 0.8
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							has_war_with = ROOT
							NOT = { has_war_with = event_target:Politcenter }
						}
						declare_war_on = { target = event_target:Politcenter type = annex_everything }
					}
			}
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { OR = { has_id = 92354 has_id = 92355 has_id = 88153 } }
				set_nationality = event_target:Politcenter
			}
			event_target:Politcenter = {
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = ROOT
					size = 1
					stockpile_ratio = 1
					army_ratio = 1
					navy_ratio = 1
					air_ratio = 1
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { OR = { has_id = 92354 has_id = 92355 has_id = 88153 } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { any_country = { OR = { exists = yes exists = no } any_unit_leader = { has_id = 92356 } } }
					}
					create_corps_commander = { name = "Evgeniy Kolosov" id = 92356 portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Portrait_Evgeniy_Kolosov.dds" traits = { politically_connected } skill = 1 attack_skill = 1 defense_skill = 1 planning_skill = 1 logistics_skill = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { any_country = { OR = { exists = yes exists = no } any_unit_leader = { has_id = 92357 } } }
					}
					create_corps_commander = { name = "Nikolay Kalashnikov" id = 92357 portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Portrait_Nikolay_Kalashnikov.dds" traits = { politically_connected } skill = 1 attack_skill = 1 defense_skill = 1 planning_skill = 1 logistics_skill = 1 }
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = unrecognized_states
							value = ROOT.id
						}
					}
					set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment_great_war
					amount = 3000
					producer = RUS
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 500
					producer = RUS
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = RGR } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = RGR
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = BKL } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = BKL
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = RUS } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = RUS
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Partiynaya druzjina"
					regiments = {
						militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					}
					support = {
					}
					is_locked = no

							owner = CONTROLLER
						}
						create_unit = {

# Разоружение чехословацкого легиона (Сибирь)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.74
	title = rcw_usfev.74.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.74.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_czechoslovakians
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.74.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_stability < 0.4
						check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party < 0.15 }
					}
					NOT = { has_global_flag = RCW_Politcenter_fired }
				}
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.75 days = 1 }
				else = {
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona"
					}
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Dal'niy Vostok"
					}
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e"
					}
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Kuban'"
					}
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Krym"
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment_great_war
						amount = 15000
						producer = RUS
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = support_equipment
						amount = 1500
						producer = RUS
					}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = global.RCW_green_var_Siberia
						value = -1
					}
				}
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberalism popularity = -0.1 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.1 }
			add_war_support = 0.1
			add_stability = 0.2
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = 0.2
			add_war_support = 0.1
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberalism popularity = -0.1 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.1 }
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Dal'niy Vostok"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Kuban'"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Krym"
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment_great_war
				amount = 15000
				producer = RUS
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = support_equipment
				amount = 1500
				producer = RUS
			}
		}
	}
}
# Второй чехословацкий мятеж (Сибирь; Политцентр)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.75
	title = rcw_usfev.75.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.75.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rcw_czech_uprising
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = RCW_Politcenter_fired
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.75.a
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.RCW_green_var_Siberia
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB }
				create_country_leader = { name = "Florian Fyodorovich" desc = "RUS_Florian_Fyodorovich_DESC" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Florian_Fyodorovich.dds" ideology = social_democracy_ideology traits = {  } }
				else = {
					create_country_leader = { name = "Florian Fyodorovich" desc = "RUS_Florian_Fyodorovich_DESC" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Florian_Fyodorovich.dds" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = {  } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { controls_state = 566 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB }
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = social_democracy
					size = 0.1
					capital = 566
					states = {
						566
					}
				}
				else = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = social_liberalism
						size = 0.1
						capital = 566
						states = {
							566
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { controls_state = 571 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB }
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = social_democracy
						size = 0.1
						capital = 571
						states = {
							571
						}
					}
					else = {
						start_civil_war = {
							ideology = social_liberalism
							size = 0.1
							capital = 571
							states = {
								571
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB }
						start_civil_war = {
							ideology = social_democracy
							size = 0.1
						}
						else = {
							start_civil_war = {
								ideology = social_liberalism
								size = 0.1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = ROOT
						OR = {
							has_government = social_democracy
							has_government = social_liberalism
						}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = Politcenter
					save_global_event_target_as = Politcenter
					set_stability = 0.9
					set_war_support = 0.8
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							has_war_with = ROOT
							NOT = { has_war_with = event_target:Politcenter }
						}
						declare_war_on = { target = event_target:Politcenter type = annex_everything }
					}
			}
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { OR = { has_id = 92354 has_id = 92355 has_id = 88153 } }
				set_nationality = event_target:Politcenter
			}
			event_target:Politcenter = {
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = ROOT
					size = 1
					stockpile_ratio = 1
					army_ratio = 1
					navy_ratio = 1
					air_ratio = 1
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { OR = { has_id = 92354 has_id = 92355 has_id = 88153 } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { any_country = { OR = { exists = yes exists = no } any_unit_leader = { has_id = 92356 } } }
					}
					create_corps_commander = { name = "Evgeniy Kolosov" id = 92356 portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Portrait_Evgeniy_Kolosov.dds" traits = { politically_connected } skill = 1 attack_skill = 1 defense_skill = 1 planning_skill = 1 logistics_skill = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { any_country = { OR = { exists = yes exists = no } any_unit_leader = { has_id = 92357 } } }
					}
					create_corps_commander = { name = "Nikolay Kalashnikov" id = 92357 portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Portrait_Nikolay_Kalashnikov.dds" traits = { politically_connected } skill = 1 attack_skill = 1 defense_skill = 1 planning_skill = 1 logistics_skill = 1 }
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = unrecognized_states
							value = ROOT.id
						}
					}
					set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment_great_war
					amount = 3000
					producer = RUS
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 500
					producer = RUS
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = RGR } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = RGR
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = BKL } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = BKL
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = RUS } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = RUS
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Partiynaya druzjina"
					regiments = {
						militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					}
					support = {
					}
					is_locked = no
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Partiynaya druzjina\" division_template = \"Partiynaya druzjina\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = CONTROLLER
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Partiynaya druzjina\" division_template = \"Partiynaya druzjina\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = CONTROLLER
					}
				}
			}

				limit = { has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona" }
				delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona" }

						name = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona"		# Elite

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.79
	title = rcw_usfev.79.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.79.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_trilateral_agreement
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = { NOT = { has_war_with = BKL } }

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.92
	title = rcw_usfev.92.t
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.92.desc
		trigger = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MON_offer_to_puppet } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.92.desc_1
		trigger = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MON_offer_to_allience } }
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_blackhundred
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.92.a
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MON_offer_to_puppet } }
			FROM = { ROOT = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_dominion = yes } }
			set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarism }
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { is_in_faction = yes } }
					random_other_country = {
						limit = { is_in_faction_with = FROM is_faction_leader = yes }
						add_to_faction = ROOT
					}
					else = {
						FROM = { create_faction = siberian_axis add_to_faction = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { clr_country_flag = MON_offer_to_puppet clr_country_flag = MON_offer_to_allience }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.92.b
		add_political_power = -50
		FROM = { clr_country_flag = MON_offer_to_puppet clr_country_flag = MON_offer_to_allience }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { has_country_flag = MON_offer_to_puppet }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.120
	title = rcw_usfev.120.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.120.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_chernov_39_s_letter
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.120.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = government_esser } }
		add_to_variable = {
			var = directory_balance
			value = -1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.120.b
		add_to_variable = {
			var = directory_balance
			value = 1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.120.c
		trigger = { has_country_flag = government_esser }
		add_to_variable = {
			var = directory_balance
			value = 3
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 999
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
}

# Оренбургская встреча
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.121
	title = rcw_usfev.121.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.121.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_orenburg_gambit
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.121.a
		if = {
			limit = { OCH = { exists = yes } }
			OCH = { country_event = rcw_usfev.127 }
			else = {
				random_list = {
					40 = {
						country_event = rcw_usfev.122
					}
					20 = {
						country_event = rcw_usfev.123
					}
					40 = {
						country_event = rcw_usfev.124
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.121.b
		add_to_variable = {
			var = directory_balance
			value = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { OCH = { exists = yes } }
			OCH = { country_event = rcw_usfev.128 }
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						country_event = rcw_usfev.126
					}
					30 = {
						country_event = rcw_usfev.125
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
}

# Ответ Дутова (Удача)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.122
	title = rcw_usfev.122.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.122.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_orenburg_gambit
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.122.a
		add_to_variable = {
			var = directory_balance
			value = -2
		}
	}
	
}

# Ответ Дутова (Нейтрал)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.123
	title = rcw_usfev.123.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.123.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_orenburg_gambit
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.123.a
		add_to_variable = {
			var = directory_balance
			value = 1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.123.b
		if = {
			limit = { OCH = { exists = yes } }
			OCH = { country_event = rcw_usfev.128 }
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						country_event = rcw_usfev.126
					}
					30 = {
						country_event = rcw_usfev.125
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
}

# Ответ Дутова (Неудача)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.124
	title = rcw_usfev.124.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.124.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_orenburg_gambit
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.124.a
		add_to_variable = {
			var = directory_balance
			value = 2
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 999
				FROM = { is_ai = yes }
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.124.b
		add_to_variable = {
			var = directory_balance
			value = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { OCH = { exists = yes } }
			OCH = { country_event = rcw_usfev.128 }
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						country_event = rcw_usfev.126
					}
					30 = {
						country_event = rcw_usfev.125
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
}

# Вести от Махина (Удача) (от Оренбурга)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.126
	title = rcw_usfev.126.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.126.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_orenburg_gambit
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.126.a
		every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88154 } set_nationality = REB }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { OCH = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Fyodor Makhin" ruling_only = yes } } } }
				OCH = {
					create_country_leader = { name = "Fyodor Makhin" desc = OCH_Fyodor_Makhin_desc picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Fyodor_Makhin.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = {  } }
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = social_liberalism
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88154 } set_nationality = REB }
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = directory_balance
			value = -3
		}
	}
	
}

# Телеграмма Дутову
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.127
	title = rcw_usfev.127.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.127.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_orenburg_gambit
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.127.a
		FROM = { country_event = rcw_usfev.122 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.127.b
		FROM = { country_event = rcw_usfev.123 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.127.c
		FROM = { country_event = rcw_usfev.124 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_government = social_liberalism
			}
		}
	}
}

# Переворот Махина в Оренбургском казачьем войске (Оренбург)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.128
	title = rcw_usfev.128.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.128.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_orenburg_gambit
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.128.a
		create_country_leader = { name = "Fyodor Makhin" desc = OCH_Fyodor_Makhin_desc picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Fyodor_Makhin.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = {  } }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberalism
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88154 } set_nationality = REB }
		FROM = { country_event = rcw_usfev.126 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 65
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { is_ai = yes }
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.128.b
		random_list = {
			96 = {
				FROM = { country_event = rcw_usfev.125 }
			}
			14 = {
				create_country_leader = { name = "Fyodor Makhin" desc = OCH_Fyodor_Makhin_desc picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Fyodor_Makhin.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = {  } }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_liberalism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88154 } set_nationality = REB }
				FROM = { country_event = rcw_usfev.126 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
			modifier = {
				factor = 999
				FROM = { is_ai = yes }
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
}

# Назначение президента РСС эсерами
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.129
	title = rcw_usfev.129.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.129.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_diterikhs_coup
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.129.a
		create_country_leader = {
		name = "Vasiliy Boldyrev"
		desc = "RUS_Vasiliy_Boldyrev_DESC"
		picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Vasiliy_Boldyrev.dds"
		expire = "1965.1.1"
		ideology = social_liberalism_ideology
		traits = { warmonger_old_general }
	}
	add_war_support = 0.05
	add_stability = 0.05
	add_political_power = -50
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.129.b
		create_country_leader = { name = "Radola Gaida" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/CZE/Portrait_Radola_Gaida_eser_ruler.dds" expire = "1953.4.15" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = {  } }
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -100
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.129.c
		create_country_leader = { name = "Victor Chernov" desc = RUS_Victor_Chernov_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Victor_Chernov.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = {  } }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberalism popularity = 0.15 }
		add_political_power = -150
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
	}
	
}

# Разрыв коалиции РСС
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.130
	title = rcw_usfev.130.t
	desc = { text = rcw_usfev.130.d_eser trigger = {check_variable = { directory_balance < -1 }}}
	desc = { text = rcw_usfev.130.d_kad trigger = {check_variable = { directory_balance > -1 }}}
	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_diterikhs_coup
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = foreign_minister_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = economy_minister_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = security_minister_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_intel_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = military_minister_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = army_chief
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.130.a
		trigger = {check_variable = { directory_balance < -1 }}
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberalism popularity = -0.15 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberalism popularity = 0.05 }
		set_politics = { ruling_party = social_liberalism }
		#set_party_name = { ideology = social_conservatism long_name = RUS_social_conservatism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_social_conservatism_kolchak_party }
		#set_party_name = { ideology = authoritarism long_name = RUS_despotism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_despotism_kolchak_party }
		#set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = RUS_fascism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_fascism_kolchak_party }
		#set_party_name = { ideology = national_syndicalism long_name = RUS_national_syndicalism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_national_syndicalism_kolchak_party }
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_ideology_leader = social_liberalism
		create_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Nekrasov" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Nikolay_Nekrasov.dds" expire = "1975.1.1" ideology = market_liberalism_ideology traits = {  } }
		create_country_leader = { name = "Alexandr Clafton" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Alexandr_Clafton.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_conservatism_ideology traits = { min_2_biased_intellectual liberal_journalist silent_workhorse } }
		create_country_leader = { name = "Victor Pepelyaev" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Portrait_Victor_Pepelyaev.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_conservatism_ideology traits = {  } }
		create_country_leader = { name = "Vyacheslav Volkov" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Portrait_Vyacheslav_Volkov.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = authoritarism_ideology traits = { min_1_supreme_ruler staunch_monarchist anti_democrat warmonger_old_general } }
		}
		clear_variable = directory_balance
		remove_ideas = RSS_disjointed_government
		add_ideas = RSS_disjointed_government_after
		add_ideas = {
			Viktor_Chernov_1
			Mikhail_Vedenyapin_2
			Dmitry_Rakov_3
			Prokopiy_Klimushkin_4
			Evgeny_Rogovsky_5
			Nikolay_Galkin_6
			Nikolay_Galkin_army_chief
		}
		load_focus_tree = Russia_Russian_state_left_directory_focus
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.130.a
		trigger = {check_variable = { directory_balance > -1 }}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberalism popularity = 0.1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberalism popularity = -0.2 }
		set_party_name = { ideology = despotism long_name = RUS_authoritarism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_authoritarism_kolchak_party }
		set_party_name = { ideology = social_democracy long_name = RUS_social_democracy_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_social_democracy_kolchak_party }
		set_party_name = { ideology = social_liberalism long_name = RUS_social_liberalism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_social_liberalism_kolchak_party }
		set_party_name = { ideology = market_liberalism long_name = RUS_market_liberalism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_market_liberalism_kolchak_party }
		set_politics = { ruling_party = market_liberalism }
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_ideology_leader = social_liberalism
			retire_ideology_leader = social_liberalism
			create_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Nekrasov" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Nikolay_Nekrasov.dds" expire = "1975.1.1" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = {  } }
			retire_ideology_leader = social_democracy
			create_country_leader = { name = "Victor Chernov" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Victor_Chernov.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_democracy_ideology traits = {  } }
				create_country_leader = { name = "Alexandr Clafton" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Alexandr_Clafton.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_conservatism_ideology traits = { min_2_biased_intellectual liberal_journalist silent_workhorse } }
				create_country_leader = { name = "Victor Pepelyaev" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Portrait_Victor_Pepelyaev.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_conservatism_ideology traits = {  } }
				create_country_leader = { name = "Vyacheslav Volkov" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Portrait_Vyacheslav_Volkov.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = authoritarism_ideology traits = { min_1_supreme_ruler staunch_monarchist anti_democrat warmonger_old_general } }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 88166 } } set_nationality = REB }
			add_ideas = {
				Vladimir_Vinogradov_1
				Pyotr_Vologodsky_2
				Ivan_Mikhailov_3
				Vladimir_Krutovsky_4
				Grigoriy_Patushinsky_5
				Pavel_Rinov_6
				Pavel_Rinov_army_chief
			}
		}
		clear_variable = directory_balance
		remove_ideas = RSS_disjointed_government
		add_ideas = RSS_disjointed_government_after
	}
	
}

# Правый переворот в РСС (частично-исторический)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.131
	title = rcw_usfev.119.t
	desc = { text = rcw_usfev.119.d_dutov trigger = { has_country_flag = OCH_will_try_to_influence_RSS OCH = { has_government = despotism } }}
	desc = { text = rcw_usfev.119.d_adm_n_dutov trigger = { has_country_flag = OCH_will_try_to_influence_RSS OCH = { NOT = { has_government = despotism } } }}
	desc = { text = rcw_usfev.119.d_adm trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = OCH_will_try_to_influence_RSS }}}
	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_diterikhs_coup
	
	trigger = {
		tag = RSS
		has_variable = directory_balance
		check_variable = { directory_balance > 5 }
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 15
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = foreign_minister_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = economy_minister_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = security_minister_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_intel_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = military_minister_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = army_chief
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = OCH_will_try_to_influence_RSS } }
		name = rcw_usfev.119.a
		set_politics = {ruling_party = despotism elections_allowed = no}
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		set_party_name = { ideology = despotism long_name = RUS_authoritarism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_authoritarism_kolchak_party }
		set_party_name = { ideology = social_democracy long_name = RUS_social_democracy_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_social_democracy_kolchak_party }

			retire_ideology_leader = social_liberalism
			retire_ideology_leader = social_liberalism
			create_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Nekrasov" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Nikolay_Nekrasov.dds" expire = "1975.1.1" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = {  } }

			create_country_leader = { name = "Alexandr Clafton" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Alexandr_Clafton.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_conservatism_ideology traits = {  } }
			create_country_leader = { name = "Victor Pepelyaev" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Portrait_Victor_Pepelyaev.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_conservatism_ideology traits = {  } }
			create_country_leader = { name = "Vyacheslav Volkov" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Portrait_Vyacheslav_Volkov.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = authoritarism_ideology traits = {  } }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 88166 } } set_nationality = REB }
			load_focus_tree = Russia_Russian_state_Kolchak_focus
		}
		clear_variable = directory_balance
		remove_ideas = RSS_disjointed_government
		add_ideas = RSS_disjointed_government_after
		add_ideas = {
			Pyotr_Vologodsky_1
			Yuri_Klyuchnikov_2
			Ivan_Mikhailov_3
			Alexander_Gattenberger_4
			Sergey_Starynkevich_5
			Nikolay_Stepanov_6
			Vasily_Markovsky_army_chief
		}
	}

		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes

				fall_2_hyper_inflation = yes
			}
			25 = {
				rise_hyper_inflation = yes
			}
			25 = {
				rise_2_hyper_inflation = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.143.b

			limit = {
				has_idea = hyper_inflation_1
			}
			remove_ideas = hyper_inflation_1

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = hyper_inflation_2
			}
			remove_ideas = hyper_inflation_2

				has_idea = hyper_inflation_3

	id = rcw_usfev.148
	title = rcw_usfev.148.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.148.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_kolchak_real_politic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #А чоб собсна нет?
		name = rcw_usfev.148.a
		ROOT = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = sazonov_cca_2 }
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		FROM = { country_event = rcw_usfev.149 }
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = {
						array = unrecognized_states
						value = FROM.id
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					THIS_country_will_be_recognized_by_PREV = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Ну а я не хочу
		name = rcw_usfev.148.b
		ROOT = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = sazonov_cca_3 }
		}
		FROM= { country_event = rcw_usfev.150 }
	}
	
}
