	id = rcw_usfev.151
	title = rcw_usfev.151.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.151.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_kolchak_finland
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.151.a
		create_wargoal = {
			type = take_core_state
			target = RUS
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.151.b
	}

}

###Царьки средней азии РСС###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.152
	title = rcw_usfev.152.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.152.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_kolchak_finland
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.152.a
		add_political_power = 100
		RSS = { ROOT = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_colony = yes } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.152.b
		RSS = {
			add_political_power = -20
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

}

###Укриана узнала о признании РСС###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.153
	title = rcw_usfev.153.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.153.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_kolchak_finland
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = RUS }
		}
		name = rcw_usfev.153.a
		create_wargoal = {
			type = take_core_state
			target = RUS
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.153.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

}

###Приморские власти отступают с Сахалина если бычат японцы###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.154
	title = rcw_usfev.154.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.154.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_kolchak_finland
	
	trigger = {
		OR = { is_former_russian_empire_settled_non_cossack_country = yes former_russian_empire_cossack_country = yes }
		controls_state = 655
		JAP = {
			OR = {
				is_justifying_wargoal_against = ROOT
				has_wargoal_against = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.154.a
		JAP = {
			transfer_state = 655
		}
		add_war_support = -0.1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.154.b
		add_war_support = 0.1
	}

}

# Унгерн дезертирует если высокий уровень капитуляции
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.156
	title = rcw_usfev.156.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.156.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_ungern
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		OR = {
			tag = BKL
			tag = BYA
			tag = SIB
			is_main_former_russian_empire_country = yes
		}
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = BKL_government_of_the_REO
			NOT = { has_focus_tree = Transbaikal_white_cossaks_focus has_focus_tree = Transbaikal_white_cossaks_late_focus }
		}
		MON = { exists = yes has_government = despotism any_neighbor_country = { any_other_country = { has_war_with = PREV has_government = communism } } }
		any_unit_leader = { has_id = 77402 }
		NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Roman Fyodorovich von Ungern-Sternberg" ruling_only = yes } }
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialism
			has_government = communism
			has_government = social_democracy
			has_government = social_liberalism
			surrender_progress > 0.69
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.156.a
		add_war_support = -0.1
		add_manpower = -2000
		every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77402 } } set_nationality = REB }
		MON = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.157 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.156.b
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		add_war_support = -0.1
		add_manpower = -2000
		every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77402 } } set_nationality = REB }
		MON = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.157 days = 1 } }
		MON = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}

}

###Унгерн в Монголии###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.157
	title = rcw_usfev.157.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.157.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_ungern_WAAAR
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.157.a
		OVERLORD = { end_puppet = MON }
		MON = {
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Roman Fyodorovich von Ungern-Sternberg"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Roman_Fyodorovich_von_Ungern-Sternberg.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = monarchism
				traits = { spirit_of_genghis warmonger_old_general }
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = authoritarism
				ideology = despotism
				size = 0.9
				states = { 970 612 }
			}
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77402 } } set_nationality = MON }
			add_ideas = territorial_expansion_law
			add_ideas = help_from_foreign_interventionists
			load_oob = MON_Ungern
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { any_unit_leader = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } }
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
			}
			BKL = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = PREV.PREV } }
			RSS = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = PREV.PREV } }
			BYA = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = PREV.PREV } }
			FER = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = PREV.PREV } }
			AMR = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = PREV.PREV } }
			PRM = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = PREV.PREV } }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { any_unit_leader = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } } }
				create_corps_commander = { name = "Alexandr Kaygorodov" id = 77447 portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Alexandr_Kaygorodov.dds" traits = { trickster guerilla_fighter career_officer cavalry_officer } skill = 2 attack_skill = 2 defense_skill = 2 planning_skill = 1 logistics_skill = 1 }
				create_corps_commander = { name = "Boris Rezukhin" id = 77448 portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Boris_Rezukhin.dds" traits = { harsh_leader politically_connected } skill = 2 attack_skill = 1 defense_skill = 2 planning_skill = 1 logistics_skill = 1 }
				create_corps_commander = { name = "Nikolay Kazagrandi" id = 77449 portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Nikolay_Kazagrandi.dds" traits = { infantry_officer organizer ranger } skill = 2 attack_skill = 3 defense_skill = 2 planning_skill = 2 logistics_skill = 2 }
			}
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = { original_tag = MON has_government = despotism }
			set_cosmetic_tag = MON_CHI
			add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.157.b
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		OVERLORD = { end_puppet = MON }
		MON = {
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Roman Fyodorovich von Ungern-Sternberg"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Roman_Fyodorovich_von_Ungern-Sternberg.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = monarchism
				traits = { spirit_of_genghis warmonger_old_general }
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = authoritarism
				ideology = despotism
				size = 0.9
				states = { 970 612 }
			}
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77402 } } set_nationality = MON }
			add_ideas = territorial_expansion_law
			add_ideas = help_from_foreign_interventionists
			load_oob = MON_Ungern
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { any_unit_leader = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } }
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
			}
			BKL = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = PREV.PREV } }
			RSS = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = PREV.PREV } }
			BYA = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = PREV.PREV } }
			FER = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = PREV.PREV } }
			AMR = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = PREV.PREV } }
			PRM = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = PREV.PREV } }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { any_unit_leader = { OR = { has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } } }
				create_corps_commander = { name = "Alexandr Kaygorodov" id = 77447 portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Alexandr_Kaygorodov.dds" traits = { trickster guerilla_fighter career_officer cavalry_officer } skill = 2 attack_skill = 2 defense_skill = 2 planning_skill = 1 logistics_skill = 1 }
				create_corps_commander = { name = "Boris Rezukhin" id = 77448 portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Boris_Rezukhin.dds" traits = { harsh_leader politically_connected } skill = 2 attack_skill = 1 defense_skill = 2 planning_skill = 1 logistics_skill = 1 }
				create_corps_commander = { name = "Nikolay Kazagrandi" id = 77449 portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Nikolay_Kazagrandi.dds" traits = { infantry_officer organizer ranger } skill = 2 attack_skill = 3 defense_skill = 2 planning_skill = 2 logistics_skill = 2 }
			}
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = { original_tag = MON has_government = despotism }
			set_cosmetic_tag = MON_CHI
			add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
			change_tag_from = MON
		}
	}
}

# Напряжение на линии соприкосновения Сибири и КОМУЧ (Соединение с Самарой/Соединение с Омском)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.158
	
	title = {
		text = rcw_usfev.158.t_1
		trigger = {
			tag = SIB
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = rcw_usfev.158.t_2
		trigger = {
			tag = CCA
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.158.desc_1
		trigger = {
			tag = SIB
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.158.desc_2
		trigger = {
			tag = CCA
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_czechoslovakians
	
	trigger = {
		RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired }
		SIB = { exists = yes }
		CCA = { exists = yes }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				tag = CCA
				controls_state = 653
				653 = {
					any_neighbor_state = { is_controlled_by = SIB }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				tag = SIB
				controls_state = 653
				653 = {
					any_neighbor_state = { is_controlled_by = CCA }
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			SIB = { has_war_with = CCA }
			CCA = { has_war_with = SIB }
		}
		SIB = { is_subject = no }
		CCA = { is_subject = no }
		URL = { exists = no }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				CCA = {
					OR = {
						has_government = radical_socialism
						has_government = communism
						has_government = social_democracy
						has_government = social_liberalism
					}
				}
				SIB = {
					OR = {
						has_government = market_liberalism
						has_government = social_conservatism
						has_government = authoritarism
						has_government = despotism
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = national_syndicalism
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				CCA = {
					OR = {
						has_government = market_liberalism
						has_government = social_conservatism
						has_government = authoritarism
						has_government = despotism
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = national_syndicalism
					}
				}
				SIB = {
					OR = {
						has_government = radical_socialism
						has_government = communism
						has_government = social_democracy
						has_government = social_liberalism
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.158.a
		if = {
			limit = { tag = CCA }
			SIB = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.159 days = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = SIB }
			CCA = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.159 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
	
}

###КОМУЧ и Сибирь ищут компромисс по границе###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.159
	title = rcw_usfev.159.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.159.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_czechoslovakians
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.159.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		CCA = { add_ideas = SIB_CCA_border }
		SIB = { add_ideas = SIB_CCA_border }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.159.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		if = {
		limit = { tag = CCA }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = SIB
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
		limit = { tag = SIB }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = CCA
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
}

###Чехословаки отказываются вести боевые действия между собой###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.160
	title = rcw_usfev.160.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.160.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_czechoslovakians
	
	trigger = {
		OR = { is_former_russian_empire_settled_non_cossack_country = yes former_russian_empire_cossack_country = yes }
		OR = {
			has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona"
			has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Dal'niy Vostok"
			has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e"
			has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Kuban'"
			has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Krym"
		}
		any_other_country = {
			has_war_with = ROOT
			OR = {
				has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona"
				has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Dal'niy Vostok"
				has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e"
				has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Kuban'"
				has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Krym"
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.160.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona"
					has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Dal'niy Vostok"
					has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e"
					has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Kuban'"
					has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Krym"
				}
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Dal'niy Vostok"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Kuban'"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Krym"
			}
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 92354 } } set_nationality = CZE }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 88153 } } set_nationality = CZE }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 92355 } } set_nationality = CZE }
		}
	}
}

###Японские генералы убираются на Родину из Сибири###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.162
	title = rcw_usfev.162.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.162.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_czechoslovakians
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = { any_unit_leader = { has_trait = japan_advisor } has_template = "Japanesen volunteers infantry brigade" }
		OR = {
			NOT = { tag = SIB }
			has_war_with = JAP
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.160.a
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = {
				OWNER = { tag = ROOT }
				has_trait = japan_advisor
			}
			set_nationality = JAP
		}
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Japanesen volunteers infantry brigade"
			}
	}
}

	}

		name = rcw_usfev.163.b
		CCA = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.164 days = 1 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.164
	title = rcw_usfev.164.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.164.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rus_entente
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.164.a
		declare_war_on = {
			target = OCH
			type = annex_everything
		}
		OCH = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.166 days = 1 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.165
	title = rcw_usfev.165.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.165.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rus_entente
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = rcw_usfev.165.a
		annex_country = { target = OCH transfer_troops = yes }
		OCH = { every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = CCA } }
	}
}

	id = rcw_usfev.167
	title = rcw_usfev.167.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.167.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_transbaikal_jap_mission
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.167.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		SIB = { OCH = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_integrated_puppet = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.167.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = national_syndicalism popularity = 0.01 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = despotism popularity = 0.01 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.01 }
	}

####Ультиматум КОМУЧ Сибири####
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.168
	title = rcw_usfev.168.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.168.desc

			limit = { RSS = { exists = yes } }
			hidden_effect = {
			RSS = {
				random_list = {
						30 = {
							country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.175 days = 1 }
						}
						60 = {
							country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.176 days = 1 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.177 days = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { SIB = { exists = yes } }
				hidden_effect = {
				SIB = {
					random_list = {
							30 = {
								country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.175 days = 1 }
							}
							60 = {
								country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.176 days = 1 }
							}
							10 = {
								country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.177 days = 1 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

###Унгерн возвращается на родину, если война ещё не проиграна###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.178
	title = rcw_usfev.178.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.178.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_ungern_WAAAR
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		tag = MON
		has_country_leader = { name = "Roman Fyodorovich von Ungern-Sternberg" ruling_only = yes }
		has_war = no
		has_civil_war = no
		any_neighbor_country = {
			exists = yes
			OR = { is_former_russian_empire_settled_non_cossack_country = yes former_russian_empire_cossack_country = yes }
			has_capitulated = no
			is_subject = no
			NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			surrender_progress < 0.4
			NOT = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism }
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.178.a
		every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77402 has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = REB }
		retire_country_leader = yes
		add_ideas = limited_monarchy_gov_form
		add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
		remove_ideas = help_from_foreign_interventionists
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Cavaleriyskaya brigada"
		}
		every_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				OR = { is_former_russian_empire_settled_non_cossack_country = yes former_russian_empire_cossack_country = yes }
				has_capitulated = no
				is_subject = no
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				surrender_progress < 0.4
				NOT = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism }
			}
			country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.179 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.178.b
		trigger = { always = no }
	}

}

###Унгерн вернулся###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.179
	title = rcw_usfev.179.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.179.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_ungern_WAAAR
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.179.a
		REB = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77402 has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = ROOT } }
		MON = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77402 has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = ROOT } }
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarism popularity = 0.02 }
		add_manpower = 2000
		ROOT = { MON = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_colony = yes } }
		division_template = {
			name = "Kavaleriyskaya Diviziya"	# Cavalry
			regiments = {
				cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				cavalry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
			}
			support = {
				recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				engineer = { x = 0 y = 1 }
			}
		}
		capital_scope = {
			create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Otryad Ungerna\" division_template = \"Kavaleriyskaya Diviziya\" start_experience_factor = 1 start_equipment_factor = 1 start_manpower_factor = 1"
					owner = ROOT
				}
		}
	}
}

				cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				cavalry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
			}
			support = {
				recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				engineer = { x = 0 y = 1 }
			}
		}
		capital_scope = {
			create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Otryad Dutova\" division_template = \"Kazachya Diviziya\" start_experience_factor = 1 start_equipment_factor = 1 start_manpower_factor = 1"
					owner = ROOT
				}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.183
	title = rcw_usfev.183.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.183.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sov_felix_VCHK
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.183.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialism
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = white_terror_idea }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = white_terror_idea
				add_idea = left_esser_terror_idea
			}
		}
		create_country_leader = { name = "Semyon Soldatov" desc = RUS_Semyon_Soldatov_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/UDM/Portrait_Semyon_Soldatov.dds" ideology = anarchist_syndicalism traits = { worker_and_peasant } }
		if = {
			limit = { CCA = { exists = yes NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT } } }
			declare_war_on = { target = CCA type = annex_everything }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_former_russian_empire_russian_country = yes
				NOT = { has_government = radical_socialism }
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				is_subject = no
			}
			ROOT = { declare_war_on = { target = PREV type = annex_everything } }
		}
	}
}

# Союз с генералами у КОМУЧа
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.191
	title = rcw_usfev.191.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.191.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_diterikhs_coup
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.191.a
		FROM = {
			create_faction = CCA_VSUR_alt
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
				leave_faction = yes
				FROM = { add_to_faction = PREV }
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
			else = {
				leave_faction = yes
			}
		}
		FROM = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.191.b
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

			factor = 0
		}
	}

		}
		name = rcw_usfev.192.b

		RVA = { country_event = rcw_usfev.193 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	option = { #Нам придётся подчиниться

			NOT = { check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party < 0.5 } }

		name = rcw_usfev.192.c

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.193
	title = rcw_usfev.193.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.193.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_diterikhs_coup
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_supp } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = rcw_usfev_193_desc_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_unite } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = rcw_usfev_193_desc_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_surr } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = rcw_usfev_193_desc_3
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.193.a
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_supp } }
			FROM = { clr_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_supp }
			every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = FROM }
			FROM = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = despotism
					popularity = 0.04
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = authoritarism
					popularity = 0.04
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = ROOT
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_unite } }
			FROM = { clr_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_unite }
			hidden_effect = {
				RSS = {
					set_party_name = { ideology = radical_socialism long_name = CCA_radical_socialism_party_long name = CCA_radical_socialism_party }
					set_party_name = { ideology = social_democracy long_name = CCA_social_democracy_party_long name = CCA_social_democracy_party }
					set_party_name = { ideology = social_liberalism long_name = CCA_social_liberalism_party_long name = CCA_social_liberalism_party }
					set_party_name = { ideology = market_liberalism long_name = RVA_market_liberalism_party_long name = RVA_market_liberalism_party }
					set_party_name = { ideology = social_conservatism long_name = RVA_social_conservatism_party_long name = RVA_social_conservatism_party }
					set_party_name = { ideology = authoritarism long_name = RVA_authoritarism_party_long name = RVA_authoritarism_party }
					set_party_name = { ideology = despotism long_name = RVA_despotism_party_long name = RVA_despotism_party }
					set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = RVA_fascism_party_long name = RVA_fascism_party }
					set_party_name = { ideology = national_syndicalism long_name = RVA_national_syndicalism_party_long name = RVA_national_syndicalism_party }
					create_country_leader = { name = "Mark Natanson" desc = RUS_Mark_Andreevich_Natanson_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Mark_Natanson.dds" expire = "1923.7.29" ideology = agrarian_communism traits = { min_1_old_guy min_1_naive_optimist isolationist_revolutionary } }

					}
				}
				ROOT = { save_global_event_target_as = INTEGRATING_COUNTRY_MAJOR initiate_verification_of_the_popularity_of_coalitions = yes capital_scope = { set_state_flag = new_capital } }
				FROM = { save_global_event_target_as = INTEGRATING_COUNTRY_MINOR initiate_verification_of_the_popularity_of_coalitions = yes }
				RSS = { save_global_event_target_as = UNITED_COUNTRY random_state = { limit = { OR = { is_owned_by = ROOT is_owned_by = FROM } } PREV = { set_state_owner = PREV } } set_cosmetic_tag = RSS_VLG_DON } #load_focus_tree = Russia_Russian_state_directory_focus
				RSS = { inherit_technology = ROOT }
				RSS = { inherit_technology = FROM }
				party_populatiry_addition_script_1 = yes
				set_ruling_party_for_uniting_country_script = yes
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.1918 hours = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_surr } }
			FROM = { clr_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_surr }
			FROM = { every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = ROOT } }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = FROM
				popularity = 0.15
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = FROM
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = FROM }
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = RSS_VLG_DON
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.193.b
		add_political_power = -25
		FROM = { country_event = rcw_usfev.194 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

		name = rcw_usfev.206.a

				add_opinion_modifier = { target = CCA modifier = sazonov_cca_2 }
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		CCA = {country_event = rcw_usfev.207}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = {
						array = unrecognized_states
						value = FROM.id
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					THIS_country_will_be_recognized_by_PREV = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Ну а я не хочу
		name = rcw_usfev.206.b
		ROOT = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = CCA modifier = sazonov_cca_3 }
		}
		CCA = { country_event = rcw_usfev.208 }
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_rcw_Nikolay2_CCA_devil_return
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = right_monarcical_reaction_right_side }
		name = rcw_usfev.214.a
		hidden_effect = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = despotism
				states = { 573 }
				size = 1
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
			}
			ROOT = { transfer_state = 573 }
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = news_n.31 hours = 48 } }
		every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88150 } promote_leader = yes }
		set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarism }
		ROOT = { save_global_event_target_as = CCA_CW_right }
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = { name = "Vladimir Kappel" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Vladimir_Kappel.dds" expire = "1953.07.22" ideology = authoritarism_ideology traits = { warmonger_old_general staunch_monarchist min_2_ideological_crusader anti_democrat } }
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = social_liberalism
				size = 0.3
				keep_unit_leaders = { 88150 }
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = ROOT
				}
				save_global_event_target_as = CCA_CW_eser
			}
			event_target:CCA_CW_eser = {
				load_focus_tree = Committee_of_Members_of_the_Constituent_Assembly_focus
				if = {
					limit = { RUS = { exists = yes OR = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism } } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = RUS
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:CCA_CW_right = {
				add_ideas = military_dictatorship_gov_form
				load_focus_tree = His_Imperial_Majesty_Military_Committee_focus
			}
		}
		
		event_target:CCA_CW_right = {
			division_template = {
				name = "Monarhicheskaya Brigada"
				regiments = {
					militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				}
				is_locked = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { CCA_CW_right_forces_temp = ROOT.CCA_CW_right_forces }
			spawn_right_units_in_CCA_CW_cycle = yes
		}
		event_target:CCA_CW_eser = {
			division_template = {
				name = "Narodnoarmeyskaya Brigada"
				regiments = {
					militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				}
				is_locked = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { CCA_CW_eser_forces_temp = ROOT.CCA_CW_eser_forces }
			spawn_eser_units_in_CCA_CW_cycle = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { event_target:CCA_CW_eser = { has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e" } check_variable = { CCA_CZE_support > 2 } }
			event_target:CCA_CW_eser = {
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit= {
						division = "name = \"1-ya Brigada Stanislava Checheka Chekhoslovatskogo legiona\" division_template = \"Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e\" start_experience_factor = 0.6 start_equipment_factor = 1 start_manpower_factor = 1"
						owner = event_target:CCA_CW_eser_forces
					}
					create_unit= {
						division = "name = \"2-ya Brigada Stanislava Checheka Chekhoslovatskogo legiona\" division_template = \"Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e\" start_experience_factor = 0.6 start_equipment_factor = 1 start_manpower_factor = 1"

					}

						owner = event_target:CCA_CW_eser_forces
					}
					create_unit= {
						division = "name = \"1-ya Brigada Sergeya Voycehovskogo Chekhoslovatskogo legiona\" division_template = \"Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e\" start_experience_factor = 0.6 start_equipment_factor = 1 start_manpower_factor = 1"
						owner = event_target:CCA_CW_eser_forces
					}

						owner = event_target:CCA_CW_eser_forces
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { event_target:CCA_CW_right_forces = { has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e" } check_variable = { CCA_CZE_support < -2 } }

						owner = event_target:CCA_CW_right_forces
					}

				}
			}

				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e"
				}

		clear_variable = CCA_CW_right_forces

		}

			size = 0.7
		}

		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarism popularity = -1 }

		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = ROOT
				}
				save_global_event_target_as = CCA_CW_right
			}
			event_target:CCA_CW_eser = {
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88150 } promote_leader = yes }

					limit = { RUS = { exists = yes OR = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism has_government = social_democracy has_government = social_liberalism } } }

						type = annex_everything

				add_ideas = military_dictatorship_gov_form

			}

# Русская Вандея
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.252
	title = rcw_usfev.252.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.252.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_long_live_the_dmitry
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { RUS = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_dead } has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here }
			NOT = { RUS = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Nikolayevich_Romanov_dead } has_country_flag = Nikolay_Nikolayevich_Romanov_is_here }
			NOT = { RUS = { has_country_flag = Mikhail_Alexandrovich_Romanov_dead } has_country_flag = Mikhail_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here }
			NOT = { RUS = { has_country_flag = Kirill_Vladimirovich_Romanov_dead } has_country_flag = Kirill_Vladimirovich_Romanov_is_here }
			NOT = { RUS = { has_country_flag = Dmitriy_Pavlovich_Romanov_dead } has_country_flag = Dmitriy_Pavlovich_Romanov_is_here }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.252.a #Дело Романовых продолжается
		if = {
			limit = { RUS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_dead } } NOT = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { any_country = { has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay II Romanov" ruling_only = yes } } }
					NOT = { any_country = { has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Alexandrovich Romanov" ruling_only = yes } } }
				}
				random_list = {
					70 = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.254 days = 1 } }
					30 = { }
				}
				else = {
					random_other_country = {
						limit = { OR = { has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay II Romanov" ruling_only = yes } has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Alexandrovich Romanov" ruling_only = yes } has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here any_unit_leader = { has_id = 77401 } } }
						country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.253 days = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RUS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Nikolayevich_Romanov_dead } } NOT = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Nikolayevich_Romanov_is_here } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { any_country = { has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay III Romanov" ruling_only = yes } } }
					NOT = { any_country = { has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Nikolaevich Romanov" ruling_only = yes } } }
				}
				random_list = {
					70 = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.255 days = 1 } }
					30 = { }
				}
				else = {
					random_other_country = {
						limit = { OR = { has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay III Romanov" ruling_only = yes } has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Nikolaevich Romanov" ruling_only = yes } has_country_flag = Nikolay_Nikolayevich_Romanov_is_here any_unit_leader = { has_id = 76836 } } }
						country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.253 days = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RUS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Mikhail_Alexandrovich_Romanov_dead } } NOT = { has_country_flag = Mikhail_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { any_country = { has_country_leader = { name = "Mikhail II Romanov" ruling_only = yes } } }
					NOT = { any_country = { has_country_leader = { name = "Mikhail Alexandrovich Romanov" ruling_only = yes } } }
				}
				random_list = {
					70 = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.256 days = 1 } }
					30 = { }
				}
				else = {
					random_other_country = {
						limit = { OR = { has_country_leader = { name = "Mikhail II Romanov" ruling_only = yes } has_country_leader = { name = "Mikhail Alexandrovich Romanov" ruling_only = yes } has_country_flag = Mikhail_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here any_unit_leader = { has_id = 77410 } } }
						country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.253 days = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RUS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Kirill_Vladimirovich_Romanov_dead } } NOT = { has_country_flag = Kirill_Vladimirovich_Romanov_is_here } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { any_country = { has_country_leader = { name = "Kirill I Romanov" ruling_only = yes } } }

				}

		if = {

						country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.253 days = 1 }
					}
				}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.254
	title = rcw_usfev.254.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.254.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_long_live_the_dmitry
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.254.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarism popularity = 0.03 }
		FROM = { clr_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here }
		set_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here
		FROM = { remove_ideas = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_army_chief }
		FROM = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 77401 } set_nationality = ROOT } }
		REB = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 77401 } set_nationality = ROOT } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay II Romanov" ruling_only = yes }
						has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Alexandrovich Romanov" ruling_only = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { original_tag = CCA } }
				FROM = {
					transfer_units_fraction= {
						target = ROOT
						size = 1
						stockpile_ratio = 1
						army_ratio = 1
						navy_ratio = 1
						air_ratio = 1
					}
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = FROM
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				else = { FROM = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_puppet = yes retire_country_leader = yes } }
			}
			else = {
				hidden_effect = {
					every_country = {
						limit = { OR = { has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay II Romanov" ruling_only = no } has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Alexandrovich Romanov" ruling_only = no } } }
						retire_ideology_leader = authoritarism
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = BKL_Burnatcom_was_disbanded }
			custom_effect_tooltip = rcw_usfev_331_desc_tt
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.331.a
		remove_ideas = BKL_balagat_movement
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = BKL_balagat_movement_1 }
		country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.332 days = 60 }
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.331.b
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BKL_balagat_movement }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BKL_balagat_movement
				add_idea = BKL_balagat_movement_1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.331.c
		remove_ideas = BKL_balagat_movement
		add_timed_idea = { idea = BKL_balagat_movement days = 180 }
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = BKL_Burnatcom_was_disbanded }
		name = rcw_usfev.331.d
		BYA = {
			transfer_state = 564
		}
		puppet = BYA
		BYA = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarism
			}
			set_popularities = {
				authoritarism = 100
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = rcw_usfev.339
	title = rcw_usfev.339.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.339.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_bkl_transbaikal_crisis
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.339.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = BKL_agreement_with_the_siberian_government }
			FROM = {
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_offensive_war_with = ROOT }
						declare_war_on = {
							target = PREV
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_defensive_war_with = ROOT }
						ROOT = {
							declare_war_on = {
								target = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = { ROOT = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_semi_independent = yes } }
		}
		remove_ideas = BKL_confiscation_idea
		add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = -1 }
		FROM = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.340 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.339.b
		FROM = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.341 days = 1 } }
	}
}

# Восстание Толстихина (Забайкалье)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.342
	title = rcw_usfev.342.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.342.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_bkl_tolstikhin_revolt
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		tag = BKL
		is_subject = no
		has_completed_focus = BKL_provisional_regional_government
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = BKL_confrontation_to_the_siberian_government
			has_idea = BKL_confiscation_idea
		}
		OR = {
			SIB = { is_neighbor_of = ROOT is_subject = no has_war_with = RSR NOT = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism } }
			RSS = { is_neighbor_of = ROOT is_subject = no has_war_with = RSR NOT = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism } }
		}
		has_civil_war = no
		has_war = yes
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			has_idea = BKL_confiscation_idea
			has_completed_focus = BKL_cargo_requisition
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				has_war_with = SIB
				has_war_with = RSS
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.342.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberalism popularity = -0.2 }
		create_dynamic_country = {
			original_tag = BKL
			save_global_event_target_as = BKL_CW
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { BKL = { has_idea = peasant_and_land_and_bread_question_0_25 } }
					add_ideas = peasant_and_land_and_bread_question_0_25
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { BKL = { has_idea = peasant_and_land_and_bread_question_0_5 } }
					add_ideas = peasant_and_land_and_bread_question_0_5
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { BKL = { has_idea = peasant_and_land_and_bread_question } }
					add_ideas = peasant_and_land_and_bread_question
				}
				add_random_ministers = yes
				add_random_ministers = yes
				create_country_leader = { name = "Ivan Tolstikhin" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/BKL/Portrait_Ivan_Tolstikhin.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = {  } }
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { controls_state = 1208 owns_state = 1208 } }
					transfer_state = 1208
					else = {
						ROOT = {
							random_owned_controlled_state = {
								event_target:BKL_CW = { transfer_state = PREV }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				load_focus_tree = Transbaikal_Chita_eser_focus
				set_country_flag = BKL_not_white_cossaks_focus
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_liberalism
					election_frequency = 36
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					social_liberalism = 100
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
			add_civil_war_target = ROOT
		}
		transfer_units_fraction= {
			target = event_target:BKL_CW
			size = 0.2
			stockpile_ratio = 0.2
			army_ratio = 0.2
			navy_ratio = 0
			air_ratio = 0
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
				NOT = { has_id = 28158 has_id = 28159 has_id = 28160 }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { NOT = { tag = SIB tag = RSS } NOT = { has_war_with = event_target:BKL_CW } has_war_with = BKL }
			event_target:BKL_CW = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PREV
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { any_other_country = { OR = { tag = RSS tag = SIB } is_subject = no has_war_with = RSR NOT = { has_government = communism } } }
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { OR = { tag = RSS tag = SIB } is_subject = no has_war_with = RSR NOT = { has_government = communism } }
				country_event = rcw_usfev.351
			}
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = { OR = { has_id = 28158 has_id = 28159 has_id = 28160 } }
			set_nationality = event_target:BKL_CW
		}
		event_target:BKL_CW = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_id = 28158 has_id = 28159 has_id = 28160 } }
				set_nationality = ROOT
			}
		}
		clear_global_event_target = BKL_CW
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.342.b
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberalism popularity = -0.2 }
		create_dynamic_country = {
			original_tag = BKL
			save_global_event_target_as = BKL_CW
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { BKL = { has_idea = peasant_and_land_and_bread_question_0_25 } }
					add_ideas = peasant_and_land_and_bread_question_0_25
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { BKL = { has_idea = peasant_and_land_and_bread_question_0_5 } }
					add_ideas = peasant_and_land_and_bread_question_0_5
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { BKL = { has_idea = peasant_and_land_and_bread_question } }
					add_ideas = peasant_and_land_and_bread_question
				}
				add_random_ministers = yes
				add_random_ministers = yes
				create_country_leader = { name = "Ivan Tolstikhin" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/BKL/Portrait_Ivan_Tolstikhin.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = {  } }
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { controls_state = 1208 owns_state = 1208 } }
					transfer_state = 1208
					else = {
						ROOT = {
							random_owned_controlled_state = {
								event_target:BKL_CW = { transfer_state = PREV }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				load_focus_tree = Transbaikal_Chita_eser_focus
				set_country_flag = BKL_not_white_cossaks_focus
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_liberalism
					election_frequency = 36
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					social_liberalism = 100
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
			add_civil_war_target = ROOT
		}
		transfer_units_fraction= {
			target = event_target:BKL_CW
			size = 0.2
			stockpile_ratio = 0.2
			army_ratio = 0.2
			navy_ratio = 0
			air_ratio = 0
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
				NOT = { has_id = 28158 has_id = 28159 has_id = 28160 }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { NOT = { tag = SIB tag = RSS } NOT = { has_war_with = event_target:BKL_CW } has_war_with = BKL }
			event_target:BKL_CW = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PREV
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { any_other_country = { OR = { tag = RSS tag = SIB } is_subject = no has_war_with = RSR NOT = { has_government = communism } } }
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { OR = { tag = RSS tag = SIB } is_subject = no has_war_with = RSR NOT = { has_government = communism } }
				country_event = rcw_usfev.351
			}
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = { OR = { has_id = 28158 has_id = 28159 has_id = 28160 } }
			set_nationality = event_target:BKL_CW
		}
		event_target:BKL_CW = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_id = 28158 has_id = 28159 has_id = 28160 } }
				set_nationality = ROOT
			}
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = { original_tag = BKL has_government = social_liberalism }
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Grigoriy Semyonov" ruling_only = yes } }

		}
	}

		name = rcw_usfev.349.a

			transfer_state = 564
			set_politics = {

				elections_allowed = no
			}

			}

				}

					target = BYA

				}

				}

						target = PREV

			air_ratio = 1

				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = BYA
					type = annex_everything
				}

					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = { name = "Grigoriy Khan I" desc = RUS_Grigoriy_Semenov_Khan_I_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/BKL/Portrait_Grigoriy_Semyonov_Khan_I.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = despotism_ideology traits = { inexperienced_imperialist spirit_of_genghis } }
		}
		transfer_units_fraction= {

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.351
	title = rcw_usfev.351.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.351.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_bkl_siberia-baikal_cooperation
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			FROM = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			NOT = { has_government = fascism has_government = authoritarism has_government = despotism }
		}
		name = rcw_usfev.351.a #Мы поддержим борьбу Толстихина
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT } is_faction_leader = yes }
			FROM = { leave_faction = yes }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT } is_faction_leader = no }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
		event_target:BKL_CW = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_semi_independent = yes }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

# Восстание оренбургских казаков
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.401
	title = rcw_usfev.401.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.401.desc
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_orenburg_gambit
	
	trigger = {
		has_start_date < 1917.11.7
		tag = RUS
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		OCH = { exists = no }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = OCH_revolt }
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
		NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_cossacks_were_disbanded }
		any_owned_state = { is_core_of = OCH }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 35
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			OCH = {
				transfer_state = 652
				add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
				remove_all_foreing_locked_templates_from_liberated_country = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								tag = PREV
								is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
								former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes
								has_war_with = PREV
								is_in_faction_with = PREV
							}
						}
						set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
					}
				}
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Kazach'ya brigada"
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.401.a
		OCH = {
			load_oob = OCH_cossaks
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { OR = { has_completed_focus = RUS_struggle_against_counterrevolution NOT = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus } } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = RUS
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCH_revolt
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		name = rcw_usfev.401.b
		OCH = {
			load_oob = OCH_cossaks
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { OR = { has_completed_focus = RUS_struggle_against_counterrevolution NOT = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus } } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = RUS
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCH_revolt
		OCH = { change_tag_from = RUS }
	}
}

# Второй Войсковой Круг
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.411
	title = rcw_usfev.411.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.411.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_och_vtoroy_voyskovoy_krug
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = social_liberalism
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_403_opt_c
					has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_408_opt_b
					has_completed_focus = OCH_create_commitete_of_salvation_of_motherland_n_revolution
				}
			}
		}
		name = rcw_usfev.411.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_liberalism
			}
			add_war_support = 0.05
			else = {
				add_war_support = -0.05
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_liberalism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberalism
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = Ivan_Akulinin_1 }
			}
			add_ideas = Ivan_Akulinin_1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = despotism
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_403_opt_c
					has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_408_opt_b
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = OCH_create_commitete_of_salvation_of_motherland_n_revolution }
				}
			}
		}
		name = rcw_usfev.411.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = despotism
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
			else = {
				add_stability = -0.05
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = despotism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = despotism
				has_government = social_liberalism
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_403_opt_c }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_408_opt_b }
			}
		}
		name = rcw_usfev.411.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = national_syndicalism
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
			else = {
				add_stability = -0.05
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = national_syndicalism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

# Второе появление Оренбурга
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.421
	title = rcw_usfev.421.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.421.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_orenburg_gambit
	
	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		owns_state = 652
		OCH = { exists = no }
		has_country_flag = OCH_revolt
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 225
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.01
			652 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.01
			251 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 652 = { CONTROLLER = { NOT = { tag = ROOT } has_war_with = ROOT } } }
				set_country_flag = OCH_occupied_by_whites
				652 = { CONTROLLER = { set_country_flag = OCH_occupier } }
			}
			OCH = {
				set_country_flag = OCH_second_revolt
				transfer_state = 652
				add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
				remove_all_foreing_locked_templates_from_liberated_country = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					every_unit_leader = {
						limit = { has_id = 88154 is_field_marshal = no }
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								tag = PREV
								is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
								former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes
								has_war_with = PREV
								is_in_faction_with = PREV
							}
						}
						set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
					}
				}
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Kazach'ya brigada"
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.421.a
		OCH = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
			complete_national_focus = OCH_rising_of_Orenburg_cossacks
			add_ideas = OCH_divided_host_idea
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = FRT_lack_of_control_of_field_commanders
				remove_ideas = FRT_lack_of_control_of_field_commanders_3
				remove_ideas = OCH_burnt_villages_1
				remove_ideas = OCH_burnt_villages_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = OCH_army_unification } }
				add_ideas = FRT_lack_of_control_of_field_commanders_2
			}
			add_ideas = OCH_burnt_villages_3
			set_party_name = { 
				ideology = social_liberalism
				long_name = OCH_social_liberalism_party_long
				name = OCH_social_liberalism_party
			}
			create_country_leader = { name = "Valentin Baranovskiy" desc = OCH_Valentin_Baranovskiy_desc picture = "gfx/leaders/OCH/Portrait_Valentin_Baranovskiy.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = {  } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = OCH_occupied_by_whites }
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = OCH_occupier }
				clr_country_flag = OCH_occupier
				if = {
					limit = { original_tag = UCH }
					country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.1958 hours = 1 }
					else = {
						puppet = OCH
					}
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = OCH_occupied_by_whites
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		name = rcw_usfev.421.b
		OCH = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
			complete_national_focus = OCH_rising_of_Orenburg_cossacks
			add_ideas = OCH_divided_host_idea
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = FRT_lack_of_control_of_field_commanders
				remove_ideas = FRT_lack_of_control_of_field_commanders_3
				remove_ideas = OCH_burnt_villages_1
				remove_ideas = OCH_burnt_villages_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = OCH_army_unification } }
				add_ideas = FRT_lack_of_control_of_field_commanders_2
			}
			add_ideas = OCH_burnt_villages_3
			set_party_name = { 
				ideology = social_liberalism
				long_name = OCH_social_liberalism_party_long
				name = OCH_social_liberalism_party
			}
			create_country_leader = { name = "Valentin Baranovskiy" desc = OCH_Valentin_Baranovskiy_desc picture = "gfx/leaders/OCH/Portrait_Valentin_Baranovskiy.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = {  } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = OCH_occupied_by_whites }
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = OCH_occupier }
				clr_country_flag = OCH_occupier
				if = {
					limit = { original_tag = UCH }
					country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.1958 hours = 1 }
					else = {
						puppet = OCH
					}
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = OCH_occupied_by_whites
		}
		OCH = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}

	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.436.b
		if = {
			limit = { BKL = { is_subject = no } }
			BKL = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.437 days = 10 } }
			else = {
				BKL = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.438 days = 10 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { PRM = { is_subject = no } }
			PRM = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.437 days = 20 } }
			else = {
				PRM = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.438 days = 20 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Интеграция? (сибиряки)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.446
	title = rcw_usfev.446.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.446.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_och_visit_v_omsk
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.446.a
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = SIB
					tag = RSS
				}
				NOT = { has_government = radical_socialism }
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				ROOT = { is_subject_of = PREV }
			}
			ROOT = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = PREV.PREV
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					add_core_of = PREV.PREV
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = ROOT NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT is_core_of = PREV.PREV } }
					add_claim_by = PREV.PREV
				}
				PREV = {
					annex_country = {
						target = ROOT
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_ai = no PREV = { is_ai = yes } }
					PREV = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.446.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}
	}
}

# Просьба о помощи
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.448
	title = rcw_usfev.448.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.448.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_och_orenburgskij_stanok
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.448.a
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = OCH_burnt_villages_1 }
				remove_ideas = OCH_burnt_villages_1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = OCH_burnt_villages_2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = OCH_burnt_villages_2
					add_idea = OCH_burnt_villages_1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = OCH_burnt_villages_3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = OCH_burnt_villages_3
					add_idea = OCH_burnt_villages_2
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = flag_OCH_help_villages_delay
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = OCH_subsidies_idea days = 120 }
		add_political_power = -50
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.448.b
		FROM = {
			clr_country_flag = flag_OCH_help_villages_delay
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

#Директория?
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.452
	title = rcw_usfev.452.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.452.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_och_direktoria

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.452.a
		hidden_effect = { set_politics = { ruling_party = despotism elections_allowed = no } }
		RSS = { set_country_flag = OCH_will_try_to_influence_RSS }
		hidden_effect = {
			ROOT = { save_global_event_target_as = INTEGRATING_COUNTRY_MAJOR save_global_event_target_as = INTEGRATING_COUNTRY_MINOR capital_scope = { set_state_flag = new_capital } }
			random_state = { limit = { is_owned_by = ROOT } RSS = { transfer_state = PREV } add_core_of = RSS }
			RSS = { save_global_event_target_as = UNITED_COUNTRY set_cosmetic_tag = RSS_All_russian_provisional_government load_focus_tree = Russia_Russian_state_directory_focus }
			RSS = { inherit_technology = ROOT }
			party_populatiry_addition_script_1 = yes
			set_ruling_party_for_uniting_country_script = yes
			country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.1919 hours = 1 }
			
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = Dmitriy_Pavlovich_Romanov_is_here }
					RSS = { set_country_flag = Dmitriy_Pavlovich_Romanov_is_here }
					if = {
						limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Dmitriy II Romanov" ruling_only = yes } }
						RSS = { create_country_leader = { name = "Dmitriy II Romanov" desc = "RUS_Dmitriy_Pavlovich_Romanov_DESC" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Dmitriy_Pavlovich_Romanov.dds" expire = "1941.3.5" ideology = monarchism traits = { inexperienced_monarch anti_democrat warmonger_old_general political_dancer } } }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here }
					RSS = { set_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here }
					if = {
						limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay II Romanov" ruling_only = yes } }
						RSS = { create_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay II Romanov" desc = RUS_Nikolay_II_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Nikolay_II_Romanov.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = monarchism traits = { inexperienced_imperialist weak_character } } }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = Mikhail_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here }
					RSS = { set_country_flag = Mikhail_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here }
					if = {
						limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Mikhail II Romanov" ruling_only = yes } }
						RSS = { create_country_leader = { name = "Mikhail II Romanov" desc = RUS_Mikhail_Romanov_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Mikhail_Romanov.dds" ideology = monarchism traits = { inexperienced_imperialist } } }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = Kirill_Vladimirovich_Romanov_is_here }
					RSS = { set_country_flag = Kirill_Vladimirovich_Romanov_is_here }
					if = {
						limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Kirill I Romanov" ruling_only = yes } }
						RSS = { create_country_leader = { name = "Kirill I Romanov" desc = RUS_Kirill_Vladimirovich_Romanov_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Kirill_Vladimirovich.dds" ideology = monarchism traits = { inexperienced_imperialist } } }
					}
				}
			
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = RUS NOT = { is_on_continent = europe is_on_continent = middle_east } }
				add_core_of = RSS
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.452.b
		set_cosmetic_tag = OCH_eastern_russia_government
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.RCW_green_var_Eastern_Union
			value = 1
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_political_power = -40
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberalism
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberalism
			popularity = 0.1
		}
	}
}

				set_party_name = {
					ideology = market_liberalism
					long_name = RSS_esser_1_market_liberalism_party_long
					name = RSS_esser_1_market_liberalism_party
				}
				CCA = { every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = RSS } }
				retire_ideology_leader = social_liberalism
				create_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Avksentev" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Nikolay_Avksentev.dds" expire = "1935.4.30" ideology = market_liberalism_ideology traits = { editor leftist_freemason doctor_of_philosophy goal } }
				set_variable = {
					var = RSS_army_independence
					value = 0
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = RSS_police_power
					value = 0
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = RSS_esser
				remove_ideas = SIB_right_oficers
				remove_ideas = PRC_government_corruption
				add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
				every_state = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { CONTROLLER = { original_tag = RSS } }
						is_core_of = RSS
					}
					remove_core_of = RSS
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = { 
						OR = {
							is_core_of = SIB
							is_core_of = CCA
						}
					}
					add_core_of = RSS
				}	
			}
		}
	}
}

# Мир с Оренбургом aka Мир с советами – заменил теги с SIB на OCH
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.491
	title = rcw_usfev.491.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.491.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_moscow_peace
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.491.a
		set_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_reds_n_Siberia_peace
		if = {
			limit = { OCH = { is_in_faction = yes is_faction_leader = no } }
			every_country = {
				limit = { OR = { tag = OCH is_subject_of = OCH } }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = RSR
					is_subject_of = RSR
				}
				capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } }
			}
			RSR = { end_puppet = PREV }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		RSR = {
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = { OR = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } } tag = OCH is_subject_of = OCH is_in_faction_with = OCH } OR = { is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes former_russian_empire_polish_region_country = yes } OR = { is_subject = no OVERLORD = { OR = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } } tag = OCH is_subject_of = OCH is_in_faction_with = OCH } OR = { is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes former_russian_empire_polish_region_country = yes } } } }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 }
						OWNER = {
							OR = {
								tag = RSR
								AND = {
									is_subject_of = RSR
									NOT = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } } }
								}
								AND = {
									is_in_faction_with = RSR
									NOT = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = 14 region = 87 region = 147 region = 148 region = 149 region = 151 region = 152 region = 154 region = 155 region = 186 region = 229 } } }
								}
							}
						}
						is_controlled_by = PREV
					}
					remove_core_of = OWNER
					remove_core_of = RSR
					PREV = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
			every_enemy_country = {

# Объединение двух стран
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.1918
	title = rcw_usfev.1918.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.1918.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sov_redarm
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hidden = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1918.a
		event_target:UNITED_COUNTRY = {
			set_popularities = {
					radical_socialism = var:radical_socialism_party
					communism = var:communism_party
					social_democracy = var:social_democracy_party
					social_liberalism = var:social_liberalism_party
					market_liberalism = var:market_liberalism_party
					social_conservatism = var:social_conservatism_party
					authoritarism = var:authoritarism_party
					despotism = var:despotism_party
					fascism = var:fascism_party
					national_syndicalism = var:national_syndicalism_party
			}
		}
		THE_GREAT_TWO_COUNTRIES_INTERGRATION_SCRIPT = yes
		random_state = {
			limit = { has_state_flag = new_capital }
			event_target:UNITED_COUNTRY = { set_capital = { state = PREV } }
			clr_state_flag = new_capital
		}
		clear_global_event_target = INTEGRATING_COUNTRY_MAJOR
		clear_global_event_target = INTEGRATING_COUNTRY_MINOR
		clear_global_event_target = UNITED_COUNTRY
	}
}

# Восстание уральских казаков
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.1920
	title = rcw_usfev.1920.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.1920.desc
	trigger = {
		has_start_date < 1917.11.7
		tag = RUS
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		UCH = { exists = no }
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
		NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_cossacks_were_disbanded }
		any_owned_state = { is_core_of = UCH }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			UCH = {
				transfer_state = 406
				transfer_state = 407
				transfer_state = 1071
				add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
				remove_all_foreing_locked_templates_from_liberated_country = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								tag = PREV
								is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
								former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes
								has_war_with = PREV
								is_in_faction_with = PREV
							}
						}
						set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
					}
				}
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Kazach'ya brigada"
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1920.a
		UCH = {
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { OR = { has_completed_focus = RUS_struggle_against_counterrevolution NOT = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus } } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = RUS
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.1930 days = 30 }
		}
		set_country_flag = UCH_revolt
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		name = rcw_usfev.1920.b
		UCH = {
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { OR = { has_completed_focus = RUS_struggle_against_counterrevolution NOT = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus } } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = RUS
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.1930 days = 30 }
		}
		set_country_flag = UCH_revolt
		UCH = { change_tag_from = RUS }
	}
}

	id = rcw_usfev.1925
	title = rcw_usfev.1925.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.1925.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1925.a
		ROOT = { UCH = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_semi_independent = yes } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1925.b
		trigger = { has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 199 } has_equipment = { artillery_equipment > 39 } has_equipment = { support_equipment > 19 } }
		ROOT = { UCH = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_semi_independent = yes } }
		UCH = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = 200
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = artillery_equipment
				amount = 40
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = support_equipment
				amount = 20
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = rcw_usfev.1928
	title = rcw_usfev.1928.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.1928.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1928.a
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = FROM }
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = FROM
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		FROM = { every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = ROOT } }
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes FROM = { is_ai = no } }
			change_tag_from = FROM
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1928.b
		FROM = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.1929 days = 1 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.1930
	title = rcw_usfev.1930.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.1930.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		RSR = { has_country_flag = UCH_revolt }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = UCH_second_revolt }
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1930.a
		REB = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { OR = { has_id = 42344 has_id = 24567 } }
				set_nationality = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_manpower = 5000
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = UCH_drujina }
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.1931 days = 10 }
				else = {
					country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.1933 days = 10 }
					country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.1935 days = 16 }
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.1934 days = 14 }
		set_country_flag = UCH_lygotnaya_diviziya
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.1936
	title = rcw_usfev.1936.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.1936.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1936.a
		add_political_power = -130
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1936.b
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = Matvey_Martynov_army_chief }
			remove_ideas = Matvey_Martynov_army_chief
			add_ideas = Vladimir_Akutin_army_chief
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = Sergey_Shepekhin_high_command }
			remove_ideas = Sergey_Shepekhin_high_command
			add_ideas = Sergey_Kirillov_high_command
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					exists = yes
					tag = CCA
				}
				OR = {
					tag = CCA
					tag = SIB
					tag = RSS
					tag = OCH
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 88155 }
					set_nationality = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Восстание астраханских казаков
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.1942
	title = rcw_usfev.1942.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.1942.desc
	
	trigger = {
		has_start_date < 1917.11.7
		tag = RUS
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		ACH = { exists = no }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = ACH_revolt }
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
		NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_cossacks_were_disbanded }
		any_owned_state = { is_core_of = ACH }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_cossacks_bolshevized }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			ACH = {
				transfer_state = 236
				transfer_state = 1254
				remove_all_foreing_locked_templates_from_liberated_country = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								tag = PREV
								is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
								former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes
								has_war_with = PREV
								is_in_faction_with = PREV
							}
						}
						set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.1943 days = 1 }
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Kazach'ya brigada"
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1942.a
		ACH = {
			load_oob = ACH_cossaks
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { OR = { has_completed_focus = RUS_struggle_against_counterrevolution NOT = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus } } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = RUS
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ACH_revolt
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		name = rcw_usfev.1942.b
		ACH = {
			load_oob = ACH_cossaks
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { OR = { has_completed_focus = RUS_struggle_against_counterrevolution NOT = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus } } } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = RUS
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ACH_revolt
		ACH = { change_tag_from = RUS }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.1950
	title = rcw_usfev.1950.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.1950.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_och_perevorot_v_orenburge

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				original_tag = ACH
				has_country_flag = ACH_reds_CW
				NOT = { any_other_country = { original_tag = ROOT exists = yes } }
				OR = { has_government = communism has_government = radical_socialism }
				RSR = { has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired OR = { has_government = communism has_government = radical_socialism } exists = yes }
			}
			has_country_flag = ACH_reds_victory_notation
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = { clr_country_flag = ACH_reds_victory_notation }
	
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = KUB_reds_victory_notation } }
		name = rcw_usfev.1950.a
		clr_country_flag = KUB_reds_CW
		if = {
			limit = { RSR = { has_country_flag = reds_want_to_create_more_republics } }
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = ACH }
				remove_core_of = RUS
				remove_core_of = RSS
				remove_core_of = CCA
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = ROOT is_owned_by = RSR }
				ROOT = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_war_with = RSR is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes is_subject = no NOT = { has_war_with = ACH } }
				ACH = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				RSR = { annex_country = { target = ACH transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
		}
		RSR = { set_country_flag = ACH_reds_victory_notation country_event = rcw_usfev.1950 }
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = ACH_reds_victory_notation }
		name = rcw_usfev.1950.b
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.1957
	title = rcw_usfev.1957.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.1957.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_orenburg_gambit
	
	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		owns_state = 407
		UCH = { exists = no }
		has_country_flag = UCH_revolt
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 225
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.01
			407 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.01
			652 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = UCH_revolt
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 407 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT } } }
				set_country_flag = UCH_occupied_by_whites
				407 = { CONTROLLER = { set_country_flag = UCH_occupier } }
			}
			UCH = {
				set_country_flag = UCH_second_revolt
				transfer_state = 406
				transfer_state = 407
				transfer_state = 1071
				add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
				remove_all_foreing_locked_templates_from_liberated_country = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								tag = PREV
								is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
								former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes
								has_war_with = PREV
								is_in_faction_with = PREV
							}
						}

					}
				}
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Kazach'ya brigada"

		}
	}

			complete_national_focus = UCH_eshe_drujiny
			complete_national_focus = UCH_kommisia
			complete_national_focus = UCH_shtab
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = UCH_vernulis_polki } }

					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 300
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = national_syndicalism
						popularity = 0.05
					}
					set_country_flag = UCH_vernulis_polki
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = UCH_lygotnaya_diviziya } }
					add_manpower = 5000
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 100
					}
					set_country_flag = UCH_lygotnaya_diviziya
				}

# Братское предложение
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.1958
	title = rcw_usfev.1958.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.1958.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1958.a
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1958.b
		OCH = { every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = ROOT } }
		annex_country = {
			target = OCH
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = OCH NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } }
			add_core_of = ROOT
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = UCH_OCH_union
	}
}
